Japan Eagerly Prepares for War: Naval Reorganization Implemented 42

Adding Battle Squadrons, Appointing Commanders, Military Department Studies Military Expansion Plans

Tokyo: In order to cope with extraordinary situations and ensure the perfection of national defense, the Navy has newly formed the Third Battle Squadron and the Third Air Battle Squadron. On June 1st, commanders and staff below were appointed and took office on the same day. The Second Battle Squadron is formed by retaining the battleships "Nagato" and "Fuso" from the First Fleet's First Battle Squadron, while the remaining "Haruna" and "Kirishima" are used. Although this reorganization is for practical combat training purposes, it is the first time that the main force battle squadrons have been placed in two units in peacetime. Furthermore, the Third Air Battle Squadron is formed with the warship "Kamui" and the Twenty-eighth Destroyer Division "Yuzuki" and "Asayuki," with the aim of ensuring the thoroughness of fleet aviation training. (1st Day Allied News)

Tokyo: The Navy Department issued an order on the 1st, appointing Vice Admiral Keitaro Hara, commander of the First Battle Squadron, as commander of the Third Battle Squadron. Rear Admiral Takashi Togari, formerly attached to the Naval General Staff, was appointed commander of the Third Air Battle Squadron. Captain Yukichi Yashiro, captain of the Tatsuta, was appointed to the Naval General Staff and also attached to the Navy Ministry. Captain Teizo Fukuda, attached to the Sasebo Naval Base, was appointed captain of the Tatsuta. Commander Yoshishige Amagai, commander of the Shiratsuyu destroyer escort, was appointed commander of the Shiratsuyu destroyer. (1st Day Allied News Agency Dispatch)

Tokyo: The government is establishing a fiscal plan based on a plan to strengthen national defense in compiling the next year's budget, hoping that the military will decide on this plan as soon as possible. Furthermore, since the content of the national defense strengthening plan is significantly related to fiscal and tax system reforms, the military's decision on the national defense plan is attracting attention from all sides. The Army Ministry and the General Staff Headquarters are currently researching the national defense plan and producing a concrete proposal, scheduled to hold a leadership meeting in mid-June to decide on the plan's outline. According to this plan, in view of international circumstances and the severe situation, the focus will be on enhancing the military equipment stationed in Manchuria, improving the second phase of air defense facilities, and preparing aviation materials, with the plan to be completed over the next three to four years. To implement this plan, the Army's national defense budget will increase by approximately 200 million yuan from next year. After this plan is decided, Army Minister Terauchi will submit it to Prime Minister Hirota and Finance Minister Baba for approval. (1st Day Allied News Agency Dispatch)

Tokyo: The Army and Navy Ministries have already begun compiling the budget in accordance with the guidelines for compiling next year's budget decided at the cabinet meeting on the 29th. It is reported that the Army's expenses will be 700 million yuan, and the Navy's expenses will be 800 million yuan, with total military expenses reaching a huge sum of 1.5 billion yuan. This will have a significant impact on Finance Minister Baba's fiscal policy and the fate of the Hirota cabinet, which is quite evident. Finance Minister Baba intends to supplement the increase in national defense spending and other expenditures by increasing national taxes. However, the budgets requested by the Army and Navy are so large that even with the implementation of maximum tax increases, the prospects are extremely difficult. Therefore, the current cabinet is said to be on the brink of danger around October of this year. (1st Day Allied News Agency Dispatch)

German-Manchukuo Commercial Agreement 50

Announced on the Same Day in Berlin and Changchun

Changchun: The Puppet Ministry of Foreign Affairs publicly announced this morning the Manchuria-Germany Trade Agreement signed in Tokyo on April 30 between the Puppet Ambassador to Japan, Xie Jieshi, and Dr. Koduki Kip, Director of the German Foreign Exchange Management Bureau, which has been approved by the governments of both countries. This agreement stipulates that each country can directly buy and sell domestic products up to 100 million yuan per year. (1st Day Allied News)

Tokyo: The contents of the German-Manchukuo trade agreement were announced on the 1st in both Changchun and Berlin. The conclusion of this agreement will open a new chapter in the economic cooperation between Japan, Manchukuo, and Germany, which is worthy of attention. The German government, with the aim of investigating the possibility of the National Socialist German Party's expansion of trade in the Far East, organized an East Asian Economic Observation Group on October 30 of last year, dispatching Chief Representative Minister Plenipotentiary Kip, Dr. Gunor, and Dr. Nozempr, to negotiate with the Japanese and Manchukuo authorities on issues such as the adjustment of trade relations between Japan, Manchukuo, and Germany, and the economic improvement between Japan and Germany. As a result of the mediation of Matsushima, Director of the Commercial Bureau of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, both sides reached a consensus on the conclusion of the German-Manchukuo trade agreement. The officials in charge of Manchukuo and Germany formally signed the agreement in Tokyo on April 30. The trade relations between Germany and Manchukuo show that Manchukuo's exports to Germany reached 53 million yuan, while imports from Germany were 12 million yuan (all in 1934), a one-sided trade favorable to Manchukuo. As for the commercial relations between Japan and Germany, Japan's exports to Germany were 19 million yuan, while imports were 109 million yuan (last year), a one-sided trade unfavorable to Japan. With the conclusion of this agreement, a triangular trade relationship can be formed between Japan, Manchukuo, and Germany, which will surely have a great effect on the mutual adjustment of trade between the three countries. Furthermore, this agreement is a business agreement between the representative of the German Exchange Bureau and the representatives of the Manchukuo authorities. (1st Day Allied News)

Main Points of Léon Blum's Speech at the National Congress of the French Socialist Party 54

Paris: Léon Blum, the leader of the Orthodox Socialist Party and the future Prime Minister, delivered a lengthy speech at the party's National Congress today. Excerpts are as follows:

Alleviating People's Suffering: Léon Blum mentioned the purpose of the future cabinet's administration, stating that "Is it possible to alleviate the people's suffering and comfort their expectations under the current system, given the frequent disasters? The establishment of a new political system is an inevitable fact. Our party has been suspending this goal and shouldering this responsibility for more than a day. However, is it possible to make sufficient preparations for the new political system in both the mental and material aspects of the people within the scope of the current system? Can we find a bridge of transition between the current society and the society we want to establish? All of these are what we want to know."

Foreign Sympathy: Léon Blum then described the impact of the victory of the left-wing Popular Front election on foreign countries, stating that "Our party's victory has been greatly comforted by the world, as evidenced by the expression of sympathy published by the Second International. We still remember that when the Second International recently held a meeting in Brussels, Belgium, all branches were greatly appreciated when they heard the news that the French left-wing Popular Front had been formed, and regarded it as a victory for freedom and democracy in Europe. When they heard the news of our party's election victory, they were even more pleased, believing that the hope for the future of the 'Labor International' of the world, and the key to its revival, is reliably guaranteed by this move. I dare say that those who harbor this hope are not only the branches of the Second International, but the hope harbored by all countries in Europe is even more profound."

Proposition of Peace: My French comrades are all loyal to their beliefs and do not hesitate to sacrifice their lives. If these people become the spokespersons of the government in the future and make a loud call from a high place, the whole of Europe will surely respond. Moreover, the peace that we advocate is fair and equal, complete and true, indivisible and effective. In a word, it is disarmament and peace. This proposition will surely be responded to. Since we are socialists of the Second International, we are more qualified than anyone else to uphold the meaning of peace, because we are loyal to our party and the Second International.

Establishing a New Political System: Our France used to have a glorious history that was recorded in historical books, but now it has reached an old age. The people of the country stick to old habits, which has become a deep-rooted problem. There is a lack of both will and consciousness for the future. A country is like a person. To encourage its vitality and revitalize its spirit, it must rely on the establishment of a new political system. Now, it is the general psychology of the vast majority of people to wait for the arrival of this new political system, not only our party, not only other proletarian political parties, not only the masses who voted for the Popular Front, but also all other people.

Executing Tasks: His conclusion said, "We should act in unison so that the promises we have made to the people can be implemented. Now we should have the courage and determination to live up to our mission. Then the victory of the Popular Front can be called the first sound of the victory of socialism." (31st Day Havas Dispatch)

Opening of the New French Parliament 55

Sarraut Cabinet Prepares to Resign, Socialist Leader to Take Over and Form Cabinet

Paris: The Sixteenth Chamber of Deputies of the French Third Republic (elected in two rounds of voting on April 26 and May 3) is scheduled to hold its first meeting at 3 PM today. It will be presided over by Charles, the oldest member of the parliament, as the provisional speaker, and several of the youngest members will be the provisional vice-speakers. Today's meeting is only to hold the opening ceremony and to elect the speaker and other officials, which is usually held on Wednesday or Thursday. In addition, the Sarraut Cabinet is scheduled to submit its resignation on Tuesday evening. President Lebrun will then entrust Léon Blum, the leader of the Orthodox Socialist Party, to form a new cabinet. The candidates for the cabinet have all been internally determined. It is expected to be formally formed around Friday of this week. According to general speculation, the new Prime Minister Léon Blum intends to reduce the number of cabinet seats and increase the number of deputy ministers in each department. Among the three parties that make up the new cabinet (i.e., the Orthodox Socialist Party, the Independent Socialist Party, and the Radical Socialist Party, as for the fourth party, i.e., the Communist Party, although it agreed to support the new cabinet, it refused to join the cabinet), three ministers without portfolio will be simply appointed. Léon Blum will serve as Prime Minister without concurrently serving as a minister. The current Minister of Justice Ta尔博斯 (Radical Socialist Party) will probably take over the post of Foreign Minister, and Representative Oliver (Orthodox Socialist Party) will be the Minister of Finance. Former Prime Minister Daladier, the leader of the Radical Socialist Party, will be the Minister of the Army, and Mayor Salangro of Lille (Orthodox Socialist Party) will be the Minister of the Interior, Representative Gemb希 (a famous lawyer belonging to the Radical Socialist Party) will be the Minister of the Navy. After the establishment of the new cabinet, it will attend the Chamber of Deputies on Monday or Tuesday of next week. The new Prime Minister Léon Blum will read out the general policy, and the Chamber of Deputies will vote to trust it. At that time, the organization of the majority party in the government will be concretized. (1st Day Havas Dispatch)

Pope's Birthday 56

50,000 People Celebrate in the Rain

After the ceremony, the Pope, wearing a red robe, ascended the high altar from the crowd and bestowed blessings on the people. Since Pope Pius IV, he is the first person to hold political power as a religious leader, as stipulated by the Treaty of Tran协和. The Pope speaks 27 languages and has traveled to England twice. British Ship "Queen Mary" Arrives in New York to a Warm Welcome 58

Took Two Days and Twenty Hours Plus, Speed Title Still Held by French Ship

Harbor Full of Ships, Skyscrapers Crowded with Cheering Crowds

(New York) The British liner "Queen Mary" departed from Southampton Port in that country at 4:34 PM on May 27, making her maiden voyage across the Atlantic. It was originally planned to break the speed record set by the French liner "Normandy" ("Normandy" took four days, three hours, and five minutes to travel from Southampton Port to New York). It passed the Ambrose Lighthouse outside New York Harbor at 12:55 PM today (British Greenwich time, which is 7:55 AM New York time), having taken four days and twenty hours plus, with no hope of breaking the "Normandy" record. (1st Day Havas Dispatch)

(New York) The White Star Line's new ship "Queen Mary" encountered heavy fog en route yesterday, losing its chance to win the Atlantic speed title. It suddenly increased its speed at night under the moonlight, reaching 31 nautical miles per hour. It arrived at the quarantine station here at 10:09 AM this morning (New York time, which is 10:09 PM Shanghai time). If it had arrived at the 白羅斯 lighthouse three hours earlier, it would have captured the record held by the French ship "Normandy." According to unofficial sources, the ship took 101 hours and 53 minutes to travel from Priest Rock to the lighthouse, while the "Normandy" took 99 hours and 14 minutes, a difference of only two hours and 39 minutes. According to official announcements, the speed of the "Queen Mary" was 29.133, while the "Normandy" was 29.94. As soon as the "Queen Mary" dropped anchor, Professor Butler, the famous president of Columbia University, boarded the ship with many others. The British Consul General also boarded the ship to congratulate Captain Sir Bredan. According to a Reuters reporter's description of the scene when the ship arrived in port, the tops of New York's skyscrapers were crowded with spectators after breakfast, many of whom brought breakfast and watched while eating. The harbor was full of ships welcoming the "Queen Mary," making it difficult for the liner to enter the port. Former New York Mayor Whelan, representing the current Mayor LaGuardia, flew over the "Queen Mary" in an airplane when it passed the Ambrose Lighthouse, broadcasting New York City's welcoming remarks. In addition, there were airplanes and various ships to welcome it. Captain Bredan immediately gave a speech in response. When the "Queen Mary" was about to reach its destination, a declaration was posted in front of the smoking room, signed by 31 famous American passengers, congratulating Captain Bredan. (1st Day Reuters Dispatch)

New Administrative Structure for Abyssinia 62

Rome Drafts Laws

Entire Territory Divided into Five Zones Under Governors

(Rome) Regarding the administrative organization of the new Ethiopian Empire, the government has recently drafted laws advocating the establishment of a governor-general stationed in Addis Ababa (i.e., the Ethiopian capital) as the highest administrative officer with full powers. Under him will be a deputy governor, a chief of staff, and two advisory bodies to assist the central government: a government committee and an advisory committee, both chaired by the governor-general, with participation from senior officials and local gentry. Except for the capital region, which is governed by the civil administrator of Addis Ababa, the entire territory is divided into five administrative zones: Eritrea, capital Asmara; Amhara (northwest), capital Gondar; Bal and Sidamo (southwest), capital Gimma; Harar (east), capital Harar; and Somalia, capital Mogadishu. Each zone will have an administrator with administrative autonomy but will be subject to the control of the Governor-General of Abyssinia. Religious affairs, laws, education, Arabic language, Islamic groups, and local customs will be allowed to continue and will be effectively protected. (Havas, 1st)

In some areas, Arab rioters threw bombs or opened fire on the military and police, who had no choice but to return fire in self-defense. In the port of Jaffa, rioters threw three bombs, and the troops retaliated, killing two rioters and wounding one. Police in Tulkarm also shot and killed a rioter. The telephone line between Nablus and Jenin has been cut. Military police have conducted searches for weapons in Arab-populated cities in both Palestine and Transjordan, confiscating many. A German Jew here has been killed. Trees and crops in Jewish residential areas have been damaged by Arabs. Jewish newspapers are extremely indignant and have issued a joint protest. Shantou Ronin Expand Smuggling Group 97

More than 60 Foreign Firms Smuggling, Inducing Chinese Merchants to Participate

Shantou Correspondence: Smuggled goods from a certain country have been flooding into Shantou since June of last year, marking its first anniversary. Over the past year, the progress of foreign smuggling firms has been rapid, growing at an astonishing pace. There are an estimated 60 such firms, not including warehouses, branches, or agencies. The number of smuggling ronin has increased from 200-300 to over 600, not including those who come and go without registering their household. At least 15 million yuan has been lost in customs duties and various special taxes collected by the Guangdong Agricultural Tax Bureau. The losses that are difficult to calculate (such as the business losses and closures of legitimate merchants) are two to three times higher. Initially, the Japanese and Taiwanese foreign firms in Shantou each operated with their own funds, but competition arose and profits were meager. Therefore, the Japanese consulate mediated and arbitrated the establishment of a Japanese Association Company. Merchants wishing to handle goods can have the Association Company handle customs declarations, cargo pickup, and warehousing. In the event of disputes or the need for forceful seizure, the transportation group organized by the Association will dispatch Taiwanese to escort the goods into the interior. There is also a beating squad dedicated to dealing with our customs enforcement teams. The internal organization is said to be very strict. In Shantou, various goods, in addition to normal customs duties, are subject to special taxes, specific taxes, consolidated taxes, and other levies, which can be several times higher than the original price of the goods, such as sulfuric acid, kerosene, refined spirits, white sugar, explosives, or monopoly goods. Even the cheapest items, such as old newspapers and old rubber shoes, are taxed at two yuan per hundred catties. However, goods sold by ronin are not subject to these taxes, so their prices are very low. As a result, they have the potential to monopolize the market not only for oil, beans, rice, and other food items, but even for cloth, matches, seafood, and other goods, which are all falling into the hands of Japanese and Taiwanese. Legitimate Chinese and foreign shops in Chaoshan have been affected, with a quarter of them closing down due to their inability to compete. However, the ronin are not satisfied with this, so they have expanded the organization of their Association Company, extending their influence deep into the interior of Fujian and Guangdong. It is reported that the expanded capital is 1 million yuan, with each share costing 100 yuan. Japanese and Taiwanese ronin own half, and the remaining half is reserved for Chinese merchants who distribute the goods to buy shares. The Association settles accounts once a month, and each share of 100 yuan can yield a dividend of 80-90 yuan in the middle of the month. During the new share offering in May, Chinese merchants who distribute smuggled goods secretly invested over 200,000 yuan, all in the names of Japanese and Taiwanese, introduced by foreign firms, and given a receipt. The Association also plans to directly charter Japanese ships in the future to transport oil beans and bean cakes from Dalian and Andong, cement, alcohol, and white sugar from Taiwan, and rice from Siam, without going through intermediaries, directly to Shantou. From then on, the import of smuggled goods will inevitably become more prevalent.

League of Nations Administrative Council's Attitude Towards China's Request for a Council Seat 98

Most Council Speakers Advocated Three Years for China and One Year for Portugal

Geneva Dispatch: The current session of the League of Nations Administrative Council has held three meetings. Although these meetings are of a routine nature, the situation has become increasingly serious due to the Italo-Ethiopian dispute. The Council's attention seems to be solely focused on that issue. Therefore, the first two meetings failed to bring it up for discussion. Furthermore, due to the Italian representative, Mr. Aloisi, the rapporteur of the Council, objecting to the inclusion of the Italo-Ethiopian dispute on the agenda, he angrily left the meeting and returned to his country. As a result, the report was not reviewed until the last meeting. The chairman, Eden, sought the Italian representative's opinion before he left. The Italian representative then expressed his agreement to the proposal to add two seats to the Council, but did not advocate for any resolution in the Administrative Council, leaving it to be resolved by the General Assembly in September. Therefore, the Administrative Council, apart from forwarding the report and the opinions of the participating representatives to the General Assembly, did not make any resolution. However, the Administrative Council's opinion can undoubtedly serve as a standard for the General Assembly to resolve the above issue. Moreover, according to the past situation of the League of Nations, any issue that can be passed in the Administrative Council will be accepted by the General Assembly. However, what remains to be resolved by the General Assembly is only the dispute of three years or one year, or the competition between China and Portugal for one year versus three years. In short, if China gets three years, then Portugal gets one year, and vice versa. Or both seats get only one year. Observing the speakers of the Administrative Council, they all sympathize with China getting three years and Portugal getting one year. For the sake of the League's justice and its universal cooperation, the Administrative Council should have this attitude. It is also the result of Guo Shi's two years of effort. We only hope that the representatives who spoke at this time will keep their promises and not make cunning attempts during the anonymous vote at the General Assembly in September. Moreover, the weakness of the League of Nations' strength has been widely seen by the world. Its prestige has been swept away, and the Covenant has become invalid, which is also generally acknowledged by public opinion. Under this circumstance, instead of attempting concrete improvements, it can only sit and wait for collapse. On our side, if we do not feel that the League of Nations is beneficial, then there is no value in participating. If we want to engage in diplomacy, we should take a proactive attitude. Therefore, we very much hope that Guo Shi will go one step further. Although we cannot hope to obtain a permanent seat on the Council, if we only obtain a one-year term with two years of effort, then we will have to compete again before the seat is even warm. It is inevitable that we will add another difficulty in a very short period of time. The reporter hereby respectfully recounts the opinions of the representatives who participated in the Administrative Council, for readers to refer to:

Chairman Eden said that the report of the Italian representative has been submitted to the Administrative Council. The report stated that the committee approved the addition of two seats, one for an Asian country and the other for a European country that does not belong to a bloc. The committee agreed to allow China to re-enter the Administrative Council in 1936. The rapporteur also proposed that this issue can only be resolved at the General Assembly and that the Administrative Council should not make a specific resolution.

The Portuguese representative, in addition to expressing his support for China's participation in the Administrative Council, said that according to the committee's proposal, Asia is equal to two seats (the reporter notes that this refers to Turkey being considered part of Asia). If one seat is given to a European country that does not belong to a bloc, then there will be a total of fourteen seats. The report seems to be inaccurate. Since the proposal is temporary in nature, then three years is inevitably too long.

The Turkish representative said that new council members should be given a three-year term, according to the usual practice of the Administrative Council. He also expressed his sympathy for China's re-entry into the Administrative Council.

The Romanian representative said that he had long hoped for China to join the Administrative Council to make up for the Administrative Council's lack of Asian representation. He felt very gratified that China could be given a seat. However, regarding the temporary seat for a European country that does not belong to a bloc, he advocated for a one-year limit.

The Soviet representative, Litvinov, said that the members of the Administrative Council had agreed to give China a temporary seat, and he was very satisfied. However, regarding the term of the temporary seat for a European country that does not belong to a bloc, it could only be stipulated as one year. Therefore, he proposed giving China three years and Portugal one year.

The Portuguese representative then further stated that he personally agreed in principle to China's three-year term, but that for this temporary measure, especially in light of the special circumstances, it could be stipulated as one year. The Portuguese representative's intention was not to give China three years while he only got one year. The Administrative Council passed the report and resolved to transfer it to the General Assembly along with the opinions of the members. At this point, an important chapter in the issue, which had undergone many twists and turns over the past two years, came to a close. (Central News Agency)

Principles of Agricultural Warehouse Loans in Anhui 99

Loan Amount of 4 Million to 6 Million, Management Office Sends Personnel to Sign Contracts

Anqing Dispatch: The Anhui Provincial Agricultural Warehouse Management Office has repeatedly sent personnel to Shanghai and Hankou to negotiate with various banks for the storage and mortgage funds required by the provincial and county agricultural warehouses. The China Farmers Bank and the China Agricultural Cooperative Loan Group have successively replied, agreeing to the loans. The Management Office, urgently needing to send personnel to various banks to sign loan contracts, has drafted nine principles for agricultural warehouse loans from specially appointed banks in Anhui Province and submitted them to the Provincial Government for approval at the 456th regular meeting. They are recorded as follows: 1. The total amount of storage and mortgage funds for agricultural warehouses in various regions is tentatively set at 4 million to 6 million yuan for the 25th year of the Republic (1936), to be lent by specially appointed banks by the Provincial Government Agricultural Warehouse Management Office (hereinafter referred to as the Office). 2. Agricultural warehouse loans from various banks, in addition to being secured by the agricultural products mortgaged in each warehouse, are also guaranteed by the Office. 3. The loan areas of various banks are determined by the Office in consultation with the banks. The loan areas for the 25th year of the Republic (1936) are as follows: 4. China Farmers Bank: Wuhu, Huaining, Tongcheng, Tongling, Lujiang, Hefei, Shucheng, Shouxian, Huaiyuan, Fengtai, Huoqiu, Xiuning, and other twelve counties. 5. Bank of China: Xuancheng, Dangtu, Hexian, Fanchang, Cangshan, Suxian, Chuxian, Dingyuan, Guoyang, Mengcheng, Lai'an, Jiashan, and other twelve counties. 6. China Agricultural Cooperative Loan Group: Fengyang, Nanling, Chaoxian, Wuwei, Wuhe, Lingbi, Qimen, Shitai, Jingde, Jixi, Shexian, Langxi, Guangde, Ningguo, Jingxian, Taiping, Qingyang, Guichi, Tianchang, Quanjiao, Haozhou, Fuyang, Yingshang, and other twenty-four counties. 7. The interest rate for agricultural warehouse loans is tentatively set at 8 per mille per month. 8. The deputy directors of provincial agricultural warehouses and the accountants and auditors of county agricultural warehouses may be guaranteed by specially appointed banks and appointed by the Office. 9. The budget for the business of provincial and county agricultural warehouses shall be approved at the beginning of each agricultural warehouse business year and reported to the Provincial Government for record. 10. The Office shall, based on the above principles, separately sign loan contracts with various banks and report them to the Provincial Government for record. 11. The funds for agricultural warehouse construction shall be borrowed from the China Farmers Bank and the provincial and local banks in accordance with the principles proposed by the China Farmers Bank, and the loan contracts shall be reported to the Provincial Government for record. 12. These principles shall be implemented after being approved by the Provincial Government Committee (May 29).

Zhangzhou's 80th Division Resolves the Bandit Gang of Zhang Heshan 100

Zhang is a Notorious Bandit from Nanjing

Zhang's Wives, Concubines, Sons, and Daughters Were All Arrested. Although Zhang Escaped, the Entire Situation Has Been Resolved

Xiamen Dispatch: Zhang Heshan, a notorious bandit from Zhangzhou, had long been entrenched in Nanjing. When the 19th Route Army was defeated and abandoned Zhangzhou, Zhang was the first to enter the city under the name of the Fujian Southern Anti-Rebel Army, obtaining more than 500 rifles and more than ten machine guns that were left behind. Although the military authorities later recovered some of them, most of them were still kept by Zhang. Therefore, Zhang's strength was the strongest among the Zhangzhou militias. Last year, the Pacification Headquarters and the Provincial Government jointly reorganized the militias throughout the province. Zhang's unit was organized into a large detachment and incorporated into the 9th Security Regiment, which was transferred to Nan'an. However, Zhang only sent his confidant Zhang Yunhan with a part of the unit. He nominally led the unit from Nanjing. Nanjing still had Zhang's main force of more than 300 men and guns, entrenched in the mountain city of Guanxi Nankeng as their base. Nankeng was especially their lair. Later, the Security Office dismissed Zhang from his position as detachment commander because he had not reported for duty for a long time. Zhang, who had actual strength and possessed huge funds, meticulously managed and dominated Nanjing, and even extended to Pinghe. Finally, the Nanjing County Government reorganized them into the Nanjing County Security Squadron, with his son Zhang Dazhou as the squadron leader. The troops were entrenched in the Shancheng area and had not been transferred. Although the authorities gave them special consideration, Zhang imposed harsh taxes and levies, and the people could not bear it. Local bullies attached themselves to him, and his power became increasingly arrogant. Whenever government troops arrived, they would retreat and evade. When the government troops left, they would return. Recently, the authorities received numerous accusations, and, considering that Zhang was growing stronger and harboring ulterior motives, they decided to resolve the situation. Qian Dongliang, the brigade commander of the 239th Brigade of the 80th Division, announced martial law in Guanxi at 7 p.m. on the 23rd, and banqueted local gentry and all members of the district office, placing them all under surveillance on the spot. He immediately dispatched troops in three routes to surround Zhang's lair in Nankeng. He first sent a battalion to Haozailin Village and Louzaicuo Village, but failed to capture Lai Changshou, an important bandit in Zhang's unit, only capturing Lai's wife. Then they arrived at Xiaoshancheng and advanced towards Nankeng. Another route went towards Xiangxi, also attacking Nankeng. Another force of one battalion went from Guanxi to Cuiwei Market, disarming the entire squadron of Zhang's unit stationed there, killing eight people including the platoon leader, and arresting Zhang Dazhou and his two wives and concubines. That night, they traveled overnight to Shancheng. Zhang Heshan's wife was arrested in Guanxi. Arriving at Shancheng, his third concubine was arrested again. The third concubine was on the run. Zhang's plainclothes team in Gezhu Market was also resolved at the same time. In addition, troops were transferred from Zhangzhou to block the Caishe area behind Shancheng. The Caishe area was where Cai Zhensheng, the leader of Zhang's accomplice "Fu Zi Hui," had set up an altar. They also copied the rear route of Nankeng from Kuiyang, forming a four-sided encirclement. However, Zhang Heshan had also taken precautions in advance, deploying sentries for more than twenty li in Nankeng. For half a month, all travelers passing through Nankeng who were not recognized by the sentries were regarded as military scouts, shot, and buried, causing many unjust deaths. Nankeng is now under a four-sided siege. Zhang Heshan is trapped in the center of the encirclement. On the morning of May 24, the gentry under surveillance in Guanxi were released, leaving only Zhang Xiangrong and Zhang Tengwan, two of Zhang's henchmen, to be escorted to Shancheng. The prisoners who were disarmed in Cuiwei Market were also escorted to the brigade headquarters. In this operation, in addition to Zhang Heshan's two wives and concubines, his son Dazhou, and two daughters-in-law being arrested, Cai Lei, Zhang's Browning squad leader, and more than a hundred other bandits and local bullies who had joined the bandits were also arrested. Feng Dengyun, the president of the Shancheng Chamber of Commerce, and Liu Jinsheng, the former president of the Chamber of Commerce, were also among them and are currently in custody. Huang Yingxin and Cai Yun, two well-known local bullies who were secretaries of the Shancheng Chamber of Commerce, were reportedly killed. Feng Fanghui is on the run. All of these were Zhang's henchmen. As for Zhang Heshan himself, he heard the news in Nankeng on the night of the 23rd and hastily tried to gather his men to resist. However, his troops did not dare to act rashly because the large army had quickly arrived from Chanchang Xiaoshancheng. Seeing that the situation was gone, Zhang led the remnants of more than forty people, along with his second and fourth concubines and Cai Zhensheng, and fled to the nearby Hengtang bamboo forest. They then joined a group of remnants who had escaped from Zhuzizhen and fled to Changjiao Yongfu. When the troops arrived at Nankeng, they only captured one bandit. Later, they learned that Zhang had fled to the bamboo forest, so they surrounded and searched the bamboo forest but did not find him. Zhang Jichun, an important henchman of Zhang, was arrested. Zhang's unit can be said to have been completely resolved at this point. However, it is said that Zhang has hidden a large number of military weapons in places such as Daxiaoshancheng Nankeng Chanchang. (May 28)

Japanese and Korean Rogues Assault and Insult Customs Officers in Bengbu 101

Demanding the Return of Confiscated Contraband Sugar

Bengbu Dispatch: Smuggling has become increasingly rampant recently. Large quantities of untaxed contraband goods are gradually being transported south. The main item being smuggled into Bengbu is sugar, which is all protected and peddled by Japanese and Korean rogues. As of the date of the establishment of the Bengbu Customs Anti-Smuggling Investigation Office on the Jinpu Railway, a total of 220 tons and 800 kilograms of sugar had been shipped from Tianjin to Bengbu, amounting to more than 4,000 bags, all stored at the freight station. Customs officers Cao Zhen, Li Jinggui, and Shao Changling, upon arriving in Bengbu, learned that the stored sugar only had freight bills but no tax bills. They immediately sealed up the contraband sugar and reported to the Customs Commissioner of the Maritime Customs, Mr. Merrell, for instructions. Subsequently, the Jinling Customs sent customs officer Zeng Xianlun to Bengbu to supervise the removal. The Customs also telegraphed the Ministry of Railways, requesting them to dispatch train cars for loading. The Ministry of Railways instructed the Jinpu Railway Bureau to comply. The Bengbu Railway Station, upon receiving the telegram from the Railway Bureau, immediately loaded all the more than 4,000 bags of contraband sugar onto train cars, which were escorted by customs officer Zeng to Shanghai at 1 a.m. on the 30th for customs processing. After this large quantity of contraband sugar was transported away, it was learned by Japanese and Korean rogues in Bengbu. At 2 p.m. today (31st), a group of five people (including three Japanese and two Koreans) were led by two locals (one Cantonese) to the freight station office of the Jinpu Railway Haxia Station to demand the return of the sugar from the station master, Wang Yanling. Wang told them that it had been transported away by customs officers. The rogues immediately requested Wang to invite the responsible customs officer to negotiate. Wang invited customs officer Shao Changling (from Tianjin) by telephone. Shao Changling, unaware that the rogues were at the freight station, accepted the invitation and went. Upon arriving and seeing the rogues, they exchanged only a few words before the Chinese and Korean rogues slapped and insulted Shao. They then punched him. Finally, the rogues raised a bench and attempted to strike Shao's head. At the time, there were seven rogues, their momentum fierce. Although they were assaulting a customs officer, no one dared to step forward to intervene. Shao, outnumbered, feared for his life and risked escaping, returning to the office to report. Cao Zhen, the director of the Anti-Smuggling Office on the Jinpu Railway in Bengbu, immediately telegraphed the Tianjin General Investigation Office to report to Director An Sier and requested the military and police authorities to provide adequate protection. At 4 p.m., the rogues returned to the freight station to demand the sugar. After Station Master Wang's vigorous explanation, the rogues left in a huff. Their arrogant behavior was infuriating. The rogues are still staying at the Jiaotong Villa. The people of Bengbu fear that these people will cause trouble and hope that the military and police authorities will severely crack down on them. (31st)

Songjiang Middle and Primary School Teachers Demand Salaries 102

The salaries of teachers in middle and primary schools in this county have always been paid monthly, without any delays. However, recently, only the salaries for February and March have been paid this semester. It is now two months overdue, and they especially hope to receive the salaries in advance before the summer vacation in June in order to make ends meet. Considering that teachers have a difficult life, how can they be allowed to be in arrears for so long? Therefore, Sun Zongkun, Tu Peiyu, Dou Yongren, Zhang Yun and other twelve people were elected as representatives to gather at the Education Bureau today and go to the County Government to petition. They were received by Secretary Shen, who promised to raise funds immediately. In addition to the salary for April, which has already been paid, he will do his best to raise the salaries for May and June. The representatives were satisfied and dispersed.

Wuxi Holds Automobile Training Class 103

In order to improve the skills of automobile drivers and instill knowledge of repair, the Highway Administration of the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Construction is holding an automobile driver training class. It will recruit 20 to 40 drivers. Applicants must have graduated from senior primary school, be between 20 and 30 years old, and hold a driver's license from five provinces and cities to be qualified. The registration period is from May 30 to June 7. The registration and examination locations will be held simultaneously in Zhenjiang, Nantong, and Wuxi. After admission, there will be two months of training. During the training period, a monthly allowance of 15 yuan will be given. After the training, they will be assigned to various lines of service, with a monthly salary ranging from 27 to 40 yuan. The examination date is set for June 8, from 8 a.m. to 5 p.m. The training date is set to begin on June 16.

Telegram Requesting Change in Cocoon Price 104

The spring silkworms in the four townships of this county have already spun their cocoons and are in good condition. The late batch is opening leaves after their major molt, but due to the shortage of mulberry leaves, demand exceeds supply, causing market prices to soar to more than four yuan per dan. Poor farmers who cannot afford to buy leaves have already abandoned their silkworms in the fields. Tang Puan and others, representatives of the cocoon industry in this county, considering this situation, have proposed that the cocoon price for this season should be determined by the Cocoon Association in accordance with the regulations of the National Economic Commission's Sericulture Improvement Association, with a maximum price of 30 yuan per dan. However, the cost of raising silkworms is significant. If the price of mulberry leaves is calculated at two yuan per dan, and the cocoon yield is calculated at a maximum of 45 jin per silkworm egg card, with each silkworm egg card consuming 900 jin of leaves, then the cost for a silkworm farmer to produce one dan of cocoons is about 50 yuan. Moreover, the leaf price for this season is as high as three to four yuan. At this cocoon price, each silkworm farmer will lose about 20 yuan for every dan of cocoons produced. Farmers will inevitably accumulate debt. The strong will take risks, and the weak will commit suicide in despair. Yesterday, they jointly telegraphed the National Economic Committee's Sericulture Improvement Association, requesting a change in the price of spring cocoons in order to maintain the livelihoods of farmers. In addition, there are a total of 263 cocoon businesses in this county. Currently, 203 businesses have reported to the Sericulture Model Zone, with 2,690 cocoon stoves.

After receiving the order, the committee ordered the Education Bureau to submit a defense within fifteen days before proceeding with the matter.

Hangzhou Implements Bureau Abolishment and Office Restructuring 107

The Zhejiang Provincial Department of Construction is changing its organization, abolishing the Highway Bureau, Water Conservancy Bureau, Commerce Bureau, and the First, Second, and Third Sections, and establishing four offices: Agriculture, Transportation, Industry and Commerce, and Water Conservancy. This took effect yesterday (the 1st). Li Deyi, the director of the Agricultural Management Office, took over the Second Section and the Fertilizer Management Office. The office is divided into three sections: Agriculture and Forestry, Agricultural Warehouses, and Fertilizer Management, as well as a Cooperative Enterprise Office. Chen Cong, the director of the Transportation Management Office, took over the Highway Bureau and the transportation portion of the First Section. The office is divided into eight sections: Road Administration, Telecommunications Administration, Navigation Administration, Engineering, Mechanical Affairs, Auditing, Materials, and Business. Zhu Huiqing, the director of the Industry and Commerce Management Office, took over the Commerce Bureau and the Third Section. The office is divided into five sections: Investigation and Statistics, Organization and Registration, Industrial Management, Commercial Management, National Loans and Special Products, as well as the Bureau of Weights and Measures. Zhou Zhenlun, the director of the Water Conservancy Engineering Office, took over the Water Conservancy Bureau. The office is divided into three sections: Engineering, Design, and Surveying. The First and Second Sections are established to handle accounting and general affairs. A total of more than 150 employees were laid off.

Ningbo Jiangdong Houtang Road Fire 108

The Shifuxing leather shop on Houtang Road in Jiangdong District was a self-built house, consisting of two three-story buildings. The family members also lived there. They had tens of thousands of assets and were quite wealthy. Recently, due to the Lingfeng incense festival, the entire family went to escape the incense, leaving only partners and apprentices in the store. Unexpectedly, around 6 p.m. on the 30th, a fire suddenly broke out on the third floor, for unknown reasons. The fire was fierce and spread to the neighboring Tongyu cigarette and paper shop, Laolixing tinplate shop, Baotaiyuan tin shop, Chen Yichang hardware shop, and Yitai sundry goods shop. Fortunately, it was during the day and close to the river. After the efforts of various fire brigades, the fire was extinguished in about an hour. A total of five three-story buildings were destroyed, with losses of no less than forty to fifty thousand yuan.

American Chamber of Commerce Cables Washington 112

Please Broadcast the Harm Caused by Smuggling in North China

The "Great American Evening Post" reports that the American Chamber of Commerce in this city has cabled Washington, urging a nationwide broadcast of the rampant smuggling in North China, which is causing significant losses to the Chinese government and foreign investors. It is widely believed that this cable will have the same effect as the cable sent by the British Chamber of Commerce in Shanghai to London, namely, that newspapers will vigorously criticize it. Although the American Chamber of Commerce's cable did not explicitly accuse the Japanese authorities of encouraging smuggling, it did ask for attention to be paid to the actions of the Japanese and the Japanese government's refusal to curb this practice. It is estimated that the loss of customs duties in Tianjin and Qinhuangdao in April reached 8 million yuan. If no measures are taken to enable the anti-smuggling teams to fulfill their duties, the losses will continue to increase. The cable also stated that foreign debts are also severely affected, and the influx of smuggled goods is greatly damaging China's entire legitimate trade. The cable was sent by Mr. Howe via the Chinese Wireless Telegraph Administration last Saturday (May 30th). Please broadcast the dangers to Chinese finance and commerce, as well as the fact that the Japanese government authorities are not taking measures to stop smuggling and are clearly unwilling to do so."

Mint's Factory Bar and Auxiliary Coins Minted in May 116

Central Mint Auditing Committee Announcement No. 34: Announcement regarding the fact that in May of the 25th year [of the Republic, i.e. 1936], the Central Mint minted Class B thousand-yuan factory bars (880 fineness) from number 56795 to number 57217, totaling 423 bars. This is announced by Chairman Kong Xiangxi on June 1st.

Hu Xiyuan Suggests Promulgating the Industrial Association Law 117

A Letter Requesting Industrial Groups to Forward to the Legislative Yuan

Newspaper Agency reports that Hu Xiyuan, general manager of the China Yaboer Electrical Appliance Factory, believes that the government has regulations for chambers of commerce, trade unions, agricultural associations, etc., allowing them to organize according to law. However, the Industrial Association Law, which is valued in modern countries, is still lacking. Yesterday, he sent letters to the Shanghai Chinese Industrial Federation, the Shanghai Machine-Made National Goods Factory Federation, the Shanghai National Goods Factory Federation, and other industrial groups, requesting them to convene a meeting to forward the matter to the Legislative Yuan to promulgate the Industrial Association Law for compliance. The original letter is as follows: "Dear Sirs, China has been an agricultural country since ancient times, so farmers account for 70-80% of the national population. Since the opening of ports, industrial products have mostly come from abroad. At that time, the so-called 'industry' in the country referred specifically to artisans engaged in handicrafts, and there was no concept of industry as such. In recent centuries, coastal areas have been opened as commercial ports, and industry has flourished, and commerce has also become increasingly prosperous. Insightful people, aware that the lack of organization in various industries was insufficient to resist foreign aggression, established the Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce during the Guangxu period of the Qing Dynasty. After the establishment of the National Government, various laws and regulations were promulgated to maintain it. Thus, there is a Trade Union Law for workers, an Agricultural Association Law for farmers, and a Chamber of Commerce Law for those engaged in sales and profits, but there are no regulations for an Industrial Association Law for those who manufacture industrial products. Taking Shanghai as an example, the organizations that manufacture industrial products include the Yarn Industry Association, the Flour Industry Association, the Match Industry Association, the Electrical Appliance Manufacturing Industry Association, etc., which are either independent in nature or join the Chamber of Commerce, but there is no legally stipulated industrial group that can be required to join. The positions of industry and commerce are different, and their interests vary. There are many past examples, too numerous to list. For example, if industry is forced to be incorporated into a commercial group, not only will the name be inconsistent, but it will also be insufficient to exert the power of the group. In Japan, there are industrial associations for industry, commercial associations for commerce, and transportation associations for the transportation industry, which lies between industry and commerce. The categories are clearly defined, and the efficiency of the groups can be fully exerted. It is no wonder that the development of its industry and commerce has shocked the world. In recent years, industry in China has flourished everywhere, and the government's promotion and encouragement have been unwavering. The future prospects are immeasurable. If there is no legally stipulated industrial group to accommodate manufacturers of industrial products, the national industrial sector will inevitably be scattered, which will be an obstacle to industrial progress. Xiyuan believes that the strict organization of the industrial sector is a matter of utmost urgency, and the formulation of laws and regulations for industrial groups is particularly pressing. However, I do not have time to study the details and procedures of industrial organization, so I cannot list them for your consideration. Your association is an industrial group, and I wonder if it is possible to invite experts to discuss and submit a proposal to the Legislative Yuan to formulate an Industrial Association Law for the organization of industrial groups, just like the Chambers of Commerce, Agricultural Associations, and Trade Unions in various provinces and cities, and regulate it by law. I humbly offer my suggestions, and I hope you will consider and decide on them with anticipation."

34 Silk Factories in This City Resumed Operations Yesterday 118

Six More Factories Expected to Resume Operations in About a Week; Trade Union Approved to Handle Silk Worker Registration

New Public Opinion reports that the local spring cocoons in Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces have all entered the market. A total of 38 silk factories are registered in this city. Those that have resumed operations yesterday include: Gongda in the Zhabei District, Dayangqiao (72 reeling machines), Hongchang (72 reeling machines), Huashun (158 reeling machines), Fengtai (416 reeling machines), Fuchang (416 reeling machines), Yufeng in Gujiawan (226 reeling machines), Hengtai (240 reeling machines), Xinglun (180 reeling machines), Yufeng on Yingpan Road (238 reeling machines), Dasheng in Tanjiaqiao (208 reeling machines), Yingfeng (240 reeling machines), Yutai in Tanziwan (200 reeling machines), Hengcang in Miaotou (200 reeling machines), Jiufeng in Yanjia Pavilion (200 reeling machines), Yuanxing on Hutai Road (208 reeling machines), Yuanji (208 reeling machines), Fuchang in Meiyuan Road, Xinzha District (240 reeling machines), Dacheng in Yutong Road (240 reeling machines), Meifeng Xieji (240 reeling machines), Baisi on Guangfu Road (208 reeling machines), Dongxiang on Chang'an Road (208 reeling machines), Jiyu on Gonghe Road (208 reeling machines), Xinchang and Yihe in the concession area (416 reeling machines), China, Changji, Xiangcheng, Shenghuo, Tongyu, Zhongxing, Qiaoyuan, Zhicheng, and Fulun (double palace) in the Hongkou District (approximately 1,800 reeling machines), Baotai and Guangyuan in the South Shanghai District (420 reeling machines). As of yesterday, a total of 34 silk factories have resumed operations, with a total of 6,852 reeling machines.

Six More Factories to Resume Operations in About a Week

Six more factories, including Tailai and Jiushun on Chang'an Road, Xinzha District, Baokang on Hengfeng Road, Hengfeng on Guangfu Road, and Lixing on Tiantong Road, Hongkou, have not yet resumed operations due to incomplete factory building and machinery arrangements. It is expected that they will resume operations in about a week. If all the silk factories in this city resume operations, there will be a total of 40 factories, an increase of seven compared to last year. However, according to silk merchants, it takes five and a half piculs of local cocoons to reel one picul of silk. The cost of each picul of dry cocoons is 100 yuan, totaling 550 yuan. Adding labor and all other expenses, each picul costs about 130 yuan, totaling 680 yuan. Deducting the by-products, which can be sold for 80 yuan per picul, it is still a loss compared to the current overseas silk price of 600 yuan. Fortunately, the factories have already sold off their stock, so they can maintain expenses, but there is no profit to be made.

Party Headquarters Approves Silk Worker Registration 119

The Shanghai Six Districts Silk Reeling Industry Union has over 10,000 silk reeling workers. In the past, due to the depression in the silk industry, many were unemployed. Now that the silk factories are resuming operations one after another, in order to stabilize the livelihoods of silk workers and compile statistics on workers' lives, a silk worker registration is being organized. A request was submitted to the Municipal Party Headquarters for approval. Yesterday, the Municipal Party Headquarters issued a reply stating, "The submission for holding worker registration, requesting review and instructions to the Silk Factory Trade Association to notify the factories to cooperate, has been noted. The Silk Factory Trade Association is ordered to comply, and a letter is sent to the Public Security Bureau to instruct the relevant branch offices to assist as appropriate. You should be informed of this reply."

Ministry of Industry Plans to Establish a Tung Oil Refining Factory in Shanghai

The Ministry of Industry, considering that the international market has a high demand for tung oil, and that general investors often take the opportunity to raise oil prices and arbitrarily manipulate the market, and that the production methods are outdated, resulting in impure oil that must be re-refined by foreign merchants before being exported, making it easy for others to monopolize, has planned to jointly establish factories in the five tung oil producing provinces of Zhejiang, Sichuan, Hunan, Hubei, and Guangxi, in order to improve production, manufacturing, and sales, and establish international credibility. The budget is set at 2 million yuan, with each of the five provinces of Zhejiang, Sichuan, Hunan, Hubei, and Guangxi contributing 300,000 yuan, totaling 1.5 million yuan, and the Ministry of Industry allocating 500,000 yuan to purchase new-style machinery to establish a large-scale oil refining factory in Shanghai. In the future, all domestically produced tung oil must be refined by the factory, and efforts will be made to control transportation and sales, so that the quality of tung oil is pure and the market price is uniform, facilitating foreign purchases. The plan is currently in active progress, and once the funds are raised, a shareholders' meeting will be held to discuss the details, survey the factory site, and begin construction of the factory buildings.

Social Affairs Bureau Starts Second Phase of Factory Inspection Yesterday 124

Divided into Sixteen Industries Including Timber, Inspection Conducted According to Regulations; Boiler Inspection Regulations to Be Implemented After Approval

Newspaper Agency reports that the Shanghai Municipal Social Affairs Bureau has a Factory Inspection Section to handle factory inspection matters. Its inspectors are all qualified after training by the Ministry of Industry. The first phase of factory inspection has long been completed. The second phase of factory inspection began yesterday, with inspections conducted according to regulations and divided into categories. The boiler inspection regulations will be implemented after approval by the Municipal Government. The details are as follows:

Divided into Sixteen Industries

The second phase of factory inspection began yesterday, divided into sixteen industries, with inspections conducted according to regulations: 1. Timber Manufacturing Industry, 2. Metallurgical Industry, 3. Machine Manufacturing Industry, 4. Electrical Appliance Manufacturing Industry, 5. Metal Products Manufacturing Industry, 6. Transportation Equipment Manufacturing Industry, 7. Soil and Stone Manufacturing Industry, 8. Power Industry, 9. Chemical Industry, 10. Textile Industry, 11. Garment Manufacturing Industry, 12. Rubber and Leather Industry, 13. Food and Beverage Industry, 14. Paper Making and Printing Industry, 15. Ornament and Instrument Industry, 16. Other Industries. Designated personnel are responsible for presiding over each industry. For example, Tian Heqing presides over the Timber Manufacturing Industry, and Li Zhongpu presides over the Metallurgical Industry. After the inspection of each industry is completed, the inspectors compile a report, providing detailed instructions on the improvements to be made to the equipment of each factory, and order the factories to take measures to improve.

Inspection Key Points

The points to be noted during the second phase of factory inspection are: 1. History of the factory: (A) Preparation period, such as the motive for establishing the factory, the person responsible for the preparation, etc. (B) Date of commencement of operation, details of commencement of operation, etc. (C) Capital, source of capital, nature, amount, etc. (D) Reorganization during the process, if so, the reasons for the reorganization and the results after the reorganization. (E) Brief history of the factory since its establishment. 2. Current situation: (A) Internal organizational situation, methods of hiring workers, and internal organization of the factory. (B) Recent business situation. 3. Technology: Names and brief resumes of specialized technical personnel, and other technical issues. 4. Raw materials: (A) Source, nature, and annual consumption of raw materials. (B) All details of raw material storage, such as stacking methods and warehouse facilities. If the raw materials are dangerous, whether they are isolated from the factory. 5. Factory building equipment: (A) Materials, style, date of construction, etc. (B) Internal layout and the capacity of each room. 6. Machinery: (A) Name of each type of machine, manufacturer, quantity of each type, date of installation, form, etc. (B) Detailed working conditions. (C) Safety equipment conditions. 7. Products: Types of products, annual output, sales destinations. 8. Detailed rules for factory safety and hygiene inspection: (A) Articles that should be forcibly implemented in the initial stage. 9. Boiler equipment.

Boiler Regulations

Regarding boiler inspection work, the Social Affairs Bureau has drafted boiler inspection regulations and submitted them to the Municipal Government for approval. They will be implemented after approval. The original plan was to start on June 1st, but it will have to be postponed.

Hu Mengjia Suffers from Anemia 129

Mr. Hu Mengjia, Director of the National Treasury Bureau of the Central Bank, suffered from anemia this spring. At first, he tried to persevere, but eventually he could not sustain his strength and sought medical treatment. After four months, he did not recover. On May 22nd, he moved into the Fumin Hospital on North Sichuan Road for treatment, staying in room 17 on the fifth floor. After being examined with X-rays, no other symptoms were found. However, his anemia symptoms worsened, so a blood transfusion was performed on the 25th, totaling 40 cc, supplied by Hu's second daughter. However, on the 27th, his body temperature suddenly rose to 40.7 degrees, so a second blood transfusion was performed, totaling 250 cc, and 250 cc of a special saline solution was injected. Unexpectedly, on the 28th, his pulse rate reached only 55 beats per minute, so 5 cc of a cardiotonic was injected, and he gradually improved. By the 29th, he suffered from urinary incontinence and his body temperature reached 40.8 degrees. On the 31st and June 1st, his symptoms were not good, and he was injected with special saline solution twice, totaling 500 cc each time. On the 31st, he also had a blood transfusion totaling 100 cc. It is possible that his condition will gradually improve.

Zhejiang Cocoons Obtained by Silk Factories in Shanghai Detained by Zhejiang Control Committee 130

Shanghai Silk Factory Trade Association Has Cabled for Release

The purchase of local spring cocoons by silk merchants from silk factories in Haining, Chongde, and other places in Zhejiang is nearing completion. The purchase of improved spring cocoons has also begun. Silk factories in Shanghai, such as Yihe, Xiangcheng, Jiyu, Xinchang, Changji, and Huasheng, were originally scheduled to start work yesterday. However, the spring cocoons obtained by the factories in various places in Zhejiang Province were detained by the Zhejiang Sericulture Control Committee, making it impossible to start work. A Newspaper Agency reporter inquired at various silk factories yesterday and heard that the Zhejiang Sericulture Control Committee detained the cocoons of the silk factories because the purchase prices were lower than the standard. It is also heard that the Shanghai Silk Factory Trade Association has cabled Zhejiang Province for release, because the Zhejiang Sericulture Control Committee stipulates the standard price of spring cocoons as 21 yuan for local cocoons and 30 yuan for improved cocoons. The factories, considering the declining prices in the European and American markets for Chinese silk, slightly reduced the price of cocoons, resulting in the detention.

Recent News from the Shanghai Municipal Gazetteer Office 132

The Second Shanghai Municipal Yearbook Will Soon Be Published; Many Ancient Sites and Documents of This City Have Been Repeatedly Searched and Discovered

The Shanghai Municipal Gazetteer Office is simultaneously advancing its three tasks of investigation, research, and compilation of historical facts of various departments in this city, without interruption. This year's Shanghai Municipal Yearbook was completely compiled in May, with more refined content, one-third more than last year's municipal yearbook, totaling about three million words. This year, the Municipal Yearbook is being printed and distributed by the Chung Hwa Book Company and is expected to be published in early August. The usefulness of the Municipal Yearbook for various circles is self-evident. The drafts of the Municipal Gazetteer have also been compiled and, after final review, will be printed. The number of people requesting information from the office is increasing daily, from the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, Land Commission, Party History Compilation Committee, Municipal Council, New Life Inspection Group, to the China Credit Information Service, the Mainland Newspaper, the Far East Magazine, bookstore graduates, lawyers, and international organizations such as the Toa Dobun Shoin and the East Asia Economic Research Institute. The office has satisfied all those seeking materials. As for the office's investigation work, it is even more thorough. Before starting any investigation, ample preparations are made, so the results are very satisfactory, and many are discoveries and attention that people at the time had not made. For example, the office's investigation of ancient sites such as Yangjinglu Cemetery, Beimiao Mingxin Temple, and Longhua Temple has yielded stone tablets, relics, and other documentary materials that have long been widely publicized throughout the city. The four large Lu Shen's Maxims Stone Tablets in the Lujia Hong Guoyu Tang were also transferred to the Shanghai Municipal Museum for preservation after the office consulted with Lu's descendants. According to the office's recent investigation of ancient sites in the Fahua district, the Song Dynasty stele "Yun Han Zhao Hui Pavilion" in Jing'an Temple still exists, but the middle part is broken. There are also stone carvings of the Fahua Sutra, handwritten by Dong Qichang of the Ming Dynasty, and stone carvings of the Diamond Sutra, handwritten by Qiao Yiqi of the Ming Dynasty, which are still preserved in the Guanyin Chan Temple on Anhe Temple Road. In addition to rubbings, the office has also asked the municipal government authorities to pay attention to their preservation.

Social Affairs Bureau Releases Statistics on Machinery Industry Accidents in March 137

Total of 75 Injuries and 1 Death

The factory inspection department of the Shanghai Social Affairs Bureau released statistics on industrial accidents in March: a total of 64 men and 11 women were injured, and 1 man died. The causes were: 1 injury from the original engine, 3 injuries and 1 death from the power transmission device, 22 injuries from power-driven machinery, 1 injury from power-driven transportation machinery, 1 injury from fire (excluding explosions), 3 injuries from hot objects and corrosive substances, 4 injuries from falls, 20 injuries from handling objects, 4 injuries from falling objects, 10 injuries from trampling and collisions with objects, 2 injuries from unknown causes, and various other causes.

News of Merchant Ship Groundings 138

Huaxin Grounded: The Huaxin, a ship owned by the Shanghai Huaxin Shipping Company, with a deadweight of 1,918 tons, a length of 239 feet, a width of 33 feet 5 inches, and a draft of 17 feet 6 inches, is currently transporting salt in Haizhou. It was decided to load enough edible salt to capacity and sail to Yuezhou, which is above Hankou. Because the water level has been rising recently and the shallow beaches on both sides are submerged, navigation is more difficult. Due to the Jiang pilot's negligence, it ran aground. The Huaxin has a deep draft and is heavily loaded. After grounding, it was impossible to get it off. The shipowner sent a telegram to Shanghai yesterday. If it cannot be dislodged during high tide, the only option is to dispatch a ship to unload the cargo before attempting a rescue.

Longshan Out of Danger: The Longshan, a ship owned by the Shi Yi Bei Company, with a capacity of 2,278 tons, a length of 299 feet 6 inches, a width of 40 feet 9 inches, a depth of 19 feet 4 inches, and a draft of 17 feet, decided to sail to Qingdao and ran aground en route. Yesterday, the Shanghai shipowner received a telegram stating that after repeated attempts and waiting for the tide, the water level has risen to 19 feet, and the Longshan has floated freely. It sailed to Xinbu yesterday, leaving three guards on board. It plans to sail back to Shanghai on Wednesday to inspect the hull.

Zhang Xiaoliang, a Prominent Construction and Timber Merchant, Passed Away Yesterday Morning 139

Zhang Xiaoliang, a prominent construction and timber merchant in this port, felt slightly unwell a few days ago but continued to work as usual. At 6 p.m. on the 31st, he still went to visit his sick wife. On his way home at around 9 p.m., he suddenly vomited, and it continued through the night. At around 8 a.m. yesterday, his children accompanied him to the Red Cross Hospital for medical treatment. At 9 a.m., after being diagnosed by a doctor, he was taken to a room to rest. Less than half an hour later, his condition worsened, and he passed away. It is said that he suffered from heart disease. Zhang was always sincere and thoughtful in his dealings with people. He would get up before dawn every day and would not rest until dusk. He personally took care of everything, big or small. He was also enthusiastic about public welfare and charitable causes. He would always respond to requests. He often said that Tao Zhu was valuable because he could both accumulate and distribute wealth. When public construction projects were in financial difficulties, they would seek help from Zhang, who would gladly help them succeed. He treated his employees with kindness and dignity like family. There were thousands of workers, but it was as if they were one person. His influence was such that everyone mourned his sudden passing. It is said that the funeral will be held at the China Funeral Home at the end of this month, on the 3rd.

Shanghai Chamber of Commerce Sends Letter to Industry Associations to Adopt Unified Party and National Flag 140

All Stores Should Have Standard No. 6 Flags

The Shanghai Chamber of Commerce sent a letter to various industry associations to promote the unified Party and National Flag: To the esteemed associations, we received a letter from the Municipal Party and National Flag Unification Promotion Committee on May 25, stating that the Party and National Flag are symbols representing the Party and the nation. Citizens must respect the Party and the nation and must respect the Party and National Flag. On national celebrations and memorial days, the national flag must be displayed to show celebration and commemoration. This is a common practice in all countries, but the citizens of our country lack recognition of the national flag, and the flags made by the people are inconsistent, which is unsightly and detrimental to national dignity, and is of great importance. The central government, in view of this, issued a clear order to unify the Party and National Flag. The party and government agencies and organizations in this city, in compliance with the central government's order, in order to rectify the city appearance and awaken the national spirit, have organized this association. Since its establishment, the association has discussed the implementation methods several times, believing that universal implementation requires door-to-door promotion, and that significant results require the assistance of agencies and organizations. It was decided that in addition to sending propagandists from this association to promote the implementation in various streets, various agencies and organizations should be notified to prepare and use the unified Party and National Flag together. Therefore, we hereby request your association to forward this letter to various industry associations, instructing all members to prepare and use the unified Party and National Flag together, in order to rectify the city appearance, awaken the national spirit, and revive the future. The association also sent the unified implementation methods to the meeting on the same day. The methods stated that the standard flag for stores is No. 6. The implementation methods are that each district will have several promotion committee members who will, together with the police station's public security bureau, persuade door-to-door, starting with the prosperous streets. It is hoped that your association will prepare the standard No. 6 flags and send promotion staff to correct the flags of the affiliated industries. If there are any flags that do not meet the standard, persuade them to replace them immediately.
