Former Clerk of the High Court, Zhu Xiongwu's Case Trial Opened Yesterday: Accused of Embezzlement and Fraud in Eight Instances, Zhu's Voice Was Hoarse, Claiming to Be Due to Excessive Stimulation 145

—All Three Defendants Detained for Further Questioning in Fifteen Days—

Zhu Xiongwu, former clerk of the Jiangsu High Court, also known as Yi Fu, during his tenure, colluded with his colleague Chen Chaozuan as his confidant and formed a private clique with his close friend Lu Wenguang. They worked together to repeatedly defraud litigants and extort money. After being dismissed by the Ministry of Justice last winter, he still lingered in the High Court, engaging in scams under false pretenses. Upon discovery, Zhu and others were arrested by name. After the investigation was completed, a public prosecution was filed against Zhu, Chen, Lu, and three others, including Chen's wife, Li Saiying, and bailiff Xu Jiaoben, for embezzlement and fraud. After a ruling by the Supreme Court, the part concerning Zhu Xiongwu was transferred to the jurisdiction of the Shanghai First Special District District Court. For the sake of procedural convenience, the original Wu County District Court handed over the remaining defendants to the First Special Court for consolidated handling. The case files have already been

sent to Shanghai, and they were separately detained. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Huang Risheng opened the court and ordered that the three defendants, Zhu, Chen, and Lu, be brought forward for questioning. The indictment against Zhu and others contained as many as eight charges, including: In the 23rd year, Wang Maishi, the wife of Wang Bingquan, appealed to the Jiangsu High Court in Qingpu due to an opium case. Lu Wenguang used the pretext of handling the case to defraud money from Wang. In April of the 24th year, Li Shannan committed a fraud case in Shanghai and appealed to the Jiangsu High Court. Lu Wenguang took charge of handling the case, but Li was still sentenced to imprisonment, resulting in the fixed amount not being paid by Li. In May of the 24th year, when the Jiangsu High Court accepted a case involving the Zai family, Zhu Xiongwu had already taken leave to return to his hometown, but he took the opportunity to defraud the parties involved by writing letters to Chen Chaozuan to inquire about the date of case assignment and the progress of procedures. Chen Chaozuan would then reply to Zhu Xiongwu,

leaking information. Last September, when the Jiangsu High Court accepted a retrial case involving Chen Yuzhang, Chen Tingzhang, and Chen Zhaochu in Shanghai due to inheritance, Zhu, on behalf of the plaintiff in the retrial, inquired with the handling clerk Ma Runde about the date of case assignment and secretly read the registers to investigate the progress of procedures, with the intention of defrauding money. Last month, when Shanghai Yu Tai Company and Wuxi Zou Chengtai Rice Mill had a debt dispute, Jiang Hongbin, the representative of Yu Tai, invited lawyers Xu Hongchang, Li Yunqing, Yang Shaoyun, and Zhou Jiapu, as well as Zou Jikang, Zou Songfan, Shao Fucheng, Jiang Dongfu, and Zhou Zhaolin, representing Zou Chengtai, to mediate at the Ji residence in Wuxi. Zhu Xiongwu was also introduced to the scene to help Jiang Hongbin,

planning everything. They dispersed only the following morning. Subsequently, Yu Tai Company applied to the Wuxi Court to register the six thousand yuan mortgage note obtained during the mediation, but it was rejected due to incomplete procedures. Fearing that the creditor's rights would be unsecured, Jiang filed a lawsuit with the court. Zhu then falsely claimed to be able to influence the handling judge, Chen Shitao, and extorted a large sum of money. In the Weng Jun case, Zhu Xiongwu used the results of the fraud to suppress the case for a long time. In the Zhu Xinfu case, Zhu instructed Lu Wenguang to contact the parties involved in the case, promising to pay after the conclusion of the case. Last December, Miao Wenye and Sheng Jiu appealed to the High Court against the Shanghai District Court Prosecutor for obstructing the national currency. Miao and others hired lawyer He Qi as their defense counsel. Zhu and He were fellow townsmen, and at He's request, Zhu lobbied the High Court. In January of this year, he went to Shanghai to meet with Miao and Ye, claiming that he could influence the case to be handled by the second criminal division,

defrauding money. As for Xu Jiaoben, it was discovered during a court-ordered search of Lu Wenguang's home that he had accepted bribes in the Zhang Xingyuan red pill case in April of the 23rd year. Li Saiying was also jointly prosecuted because she hid all the evidence of her husband Chen Chaozuan's dealings with Zhu after Zhu Xiongwu was arrested. The prosecutor then appeared in court to briefly describe the transfer of jurisdiction after the filing of the case, requesting an investigation in accordance with the law. Judge Huang then questioned Zhu and others about their age, origin, and occupation. According to Zhu, he was 44 years old, from Qianwu, and formerly served as a clerk in the Wu County District Court, then transferred to the Zhenjiang Court. In January of the 18th year, he was transferred from Zhenjiang to the Jiangsu High Court, until October 30th of last year, when he received a

department order of dismissal. On November 22nd, he left the court after handing over his duties. Chen stated that he was 36 years old, from Pujiang, and was transferred from the Wu County District Court as a clerk to the Jiangsu High Court in the 20th year. Last year, he was transferred to the Qingjiangpu High Court First Branch Court as an interrogator. Lu stated that he was 37 years old, originally from Tianjin, residing in Suzhou, serving as a lawyer's clerk, etc. Zhu's voice was hoarse and difficult to hear. When asked about the reason, he claimed that he had been deeply stimulated since the case occurred, resulting in his hoarseness. However, he did not admit to any of the accusations. Even when the court presented letters between Zhu and Chen, he claimed that he could not remember what was said in the letters due to the passage of time. Regarding the fourth charge, he even argued that it was a false accusation by the acting clerk Ma Derun under the orders of Zhu Shusheng, the president of the Jiangsu High Court. Chen and Lu also offered excuses and denied the charges. Judge Huang stated that he still needed to investigate and summon witnesses, and rescheduled the hearing for 2:00 PM on June 15th. The three defendants, Zhu, Chen, and Lu, were still sent to jail for detention.

Fish Market's Business Last Month Reached Over 800,000 Yuan 146

The Fish Guild Non-Cooperation Case Remains Unresolved, Yu Qiaqing and Others Will Meet Today to Discuss

According to Da Gong She, the Shanghai Fish Market of the Ministry of Industry has been open for two decades and business transactions have shown considerable improvement. According to statistics from the market, from the opening on the 12th of last month to the end of last month (31st), the total transaction of seafood and freshwater fish in the market reached 855,737 yuan, one jiao, and three fen. Seafood accounted for 686,316 yuan, six jiao, and nine fen, while freshwater fish accounted for 169,420 yuan, zero jiao, and four fen. Among the business operations in the previous month, the 28th was the best, with a total transaction of seafood and freshwater fish reaching 87,658 yuan, seven jiao, and eight fen. The transaction on the first day was the lowest, with a total transaction of seafood and freshwater fish reaching only 9,373 yuan, because preparations were just beginning at that time and transactions could not be concentrated. As for yesterday's business, it also reached slightly less than 50,000 yuan, it is said.

Organizing Lending: Regarding the lending to fishermen to provide relief, the Ministry of Industry has already formed a fishing industry syndicate with Shanghai banking circles, investing a total of one million yuan to engage in lending, which will only be realized at the beginning of July. During this period, the general fish shops and fishermen are at a time when the old and new are not yet connected, so the fish market will first lend small amounts of fishing industry funds. Yesterday, it was learned that this lending has already begun, and a total of 10,000 yuan has been released, it is said.

Welcome Cooperation: The thirteen fish shops in Xiaodongmen are still expressing their non-cooperation with the fish market due to disputes over lending, commission, and guarantee money, and have proposed three conditions: 1. No guarantee money will be paid when joining as a broker. 2. A branch market should be established in Xiaodongmen. 3. Loans previously issued by fish shops should be allowed to be recovered by themselves. According to fish market news yesterday, the market still welcomes all opposing fish shops to abandon their opinions and join in cooperation, and will reserve broker quotas, quietly waiting for all fish shops to join unconditionally, it is said.

Yu and Others Confer: Although the fish shops in Xiaodongmen that oppose the market have now opened for business, there are still many obstacles to joining the market. Yu Qiaqing, Zhang Shenzhi, Fang Jiaobo, Dong Yanfang, Jin Tingsun, and others, who are closely related to the fish shops, are scheduled to meet again at the Ningbo Fellow Association this afternoon to persuade the fish shops to join, it is said.

Rickshaw Association to Hold Meeting to Address the Problem of Converting Wheels 147

Circular to Members to Solicit Opinions First, Injecting Preventive Vaccination and Setting up Tea Buckets

The Shanghai Rickshaw Mutual Aid Association, in response to the Public Concession's decision to implement the conversion of rickshaw wheels on July 1st of this year, found the matter to be urgent. Given the current economic downturn and the great impact on the interests of the industry, a special emergency meeting was convened yesterday at the association's headquarters at No. 4 Yongji Lane, Liangzang Road, to discuss countermeasures. Over thirty directors, including Shen Yong, Zou Shisong, Cheng Zhongdao, and Gao Youyu, attended. The meeting was chaired by Shen Yong, and after the formalities were completed, the discussion began. The details are recorded as follows:

Resolutions

(A) Regarding how to respond to the conversion of wheels, it was resolved that: 1. Members will be notified immediately to solicit opinions. 2. Before this matter is resolved, all members must not arbitrarily change the wheels. (B) Considering the impending summer heat, it was resolved to actively carry out sanitation work: 1. Replenish various summer medicines for the free clinic. 2. Send a letter to the municipal health authorities requesting members to be injected with preventive vaccines. 3. Set up tea buckets in important areas for members to drink from. (C) Regarding the collection of overdue membership fees, it was resolved to issue a notice and then send personnel to collect the fees. (Remainder omitted)

Soliciting Opinions

Fellow rickshaw pullers, recalling last summer, when the Public Concession authorities wanted to increase our levies, this association, considering that the industry could not bear the burden, after repeated struggles and negotiations, finally achieved the goal of abolishing the increased levies. But the second difficulty has now fallen on our industry, which is that the Public Concession has decided that starting from July 1st of this year, our industry must either widen the wheels to three and a half inches wide, or convert to rubber tires. Now, the Public Concession's Announcement No. 4642 regarding this matter is copied below: "Announcement Regarding the matter of, from July 1, 1936, all rickshaws must be equipped with flat-edged iron tires that are at least three and a half inches wide, or solid rubber tires that are at least two inches wide. This announcement is specially made for public knowledge." This announcement, dated November 21, 1935, by Acting Director-General Felippo, is as serious as last year's increase in levies. After learning about this matter, this association expressed the following opinions: 1. Widening the wheels will definitely make movement more cumbersome and inconvenient. 2. Given the poor state of the economy in recent years, it will be economically impossible for the industry to replace all the wheels. 3. If we are talking about converting to rubber tires, that is even more unaffordable, because a set of rubber tires currently costs over ten yuan. 4. At the same time, rubber tires are not durable and need to be replaced every two years. How can people who earn a living by the sweat of their brow have such strength? This association has also sent a letter to the Public Concession with the above points, requesting consideration of the difficult times and exemption from implementation, but it has not been accepted. Now, the implementation period of July 1st is approaching in the blink of an eye. For the sake of seriousness, this association has specially formulated a form to solicit opinions from the industry, which will be distributed to all members. After receiving it, please indicate either "Agree", "Oppose", or "Postpone" on the form, based on your own opinion, and add a "+" sign and send it to this association for statistics to be used as a basis for negotiation. The situation is very urgent, so please do not delay. Finally, I would like to tell my colleagues that to get rid of any pain, 1. It is necessary to unite. With unity, we can have the power to resist. This is very clear. Therefore, at this critical juncture, I cannot but hope that colleagues who have not yet joined the association will join quickly, so that we can act together and increase the power of negotiation.

The Hua Dong Company's Special Reward Lawsuit Has Many Disputes, Xie Hengchuan Sues Zhang Duchen 148

Requesting a Declaration That Resolutions A and B of the Shareholders' Meeting Are Invalid. Yesterday, the Special First Court Summoned the Parties and Will Re-examine After Investigating the Case Files.

The Hua Dong Coal Mine Company was reorganized from the Jia Zai Coal Mine Company. Liu Hongniu, a director of the company, had promised to borrow 800,000 yuan for Hua Dong, with a special reward of 3 jiao per ton of coal sold in addition to the interest. Because the loan did not materialize, Gu Zonglin, the former manager, promised to raise a loan of 1 million yuan, with a special reward of 5 jiao per ton. However, as a result, the loan was not obtained, but the special reward was still extracted. The creditors, Daji Company Yan Huiyu, as well as Jincheng and Yanye Banks, considered this to be a great damage to their creditor's rights. They then hired lawyer Qiu Fenling to sue the company's general manager and directors Zhang Duchen, Hua Runquan, Xie Hengchuan, Xu Zhiyi, Bao Zidan, Tian Youfu, Lu Yinfu, Sheng Minreng, Li Bake, Wang Jianxun, He Jingfu, Li Yuliang, Liu Hongsheng, Gu Zonglin, and fourteen others at the First Special District Court, seeking affirmation that the defendants' extraction of a

special reward of 150,000 yuan in the 24th year was invalid. This case has been heard several times by the Special Court. Because the defendant Xie Hengchuan was willing to mediate, the court ordered a postponement of the hearing. It was reported in this newspaper that Xie Hengchuan recently hired lawyer Xu Jie to file a complaint with the Special First Court against Hua Dong Coal Mine Co., Ltd. and its legal representative Zhang Duchen, adding reasons and requesting a declaration that Resolutions A and B of the defendant company's Fourth Extraordinary General Meeting of Shareholders held on April 24th of this year are invalid. Yesterday afternoon, this case was opened by Judge Meng Tingke in the Fourteenth Civil Court. The defendant hired lawyer Xu Shihao to defend. According to the plaintiff's agent, lawyer Xu Jie, the Hua Dong Coal Mine Company held its Fourth Extraordinary General Meeting of Shareholders on April 24th of this year. All shareholders attended and voted to pass the following

two resolutions: A. Lawyer Qiu Fenling was entrusted by the old creditors and advance payment creditors of the Jia Zai Coal Mine to discuss the special reward issue. The company should respond to the warning letter by stating that Qiu Fenling's letter is an unwarranted interference and infringement on the company's rights. A warning letter should be sent immediately, stating that the lawyer and their clients shall be liable for compensation if any actions cause direct or indirect damage to the company. Shareholders Hua Runquan and Xie Peide seconded the motion. A public vote was taken, and Li Yuliang and Xie Peide were elected as vote counters.

The vote count showed 14 votes in favor, totaling 1,290 shares, and 1 vote against, totaling 10 shares. The 10 shares were from Xie Hengchuan, the plaintiff in this case. The majority voted to pass. B. The previous resolution on the special reward, which had been legally passed, should be maintained because some directors had created incidents afterwards, causing disputes and affecting the company's future. The original resolution should be maintained. Shareholders Xu Zhiyi moved that the original resolution should be maintained since it had already been legally passed. Shareholder Hua Runquan seconded the motion. A public vote was taken, and shareholders Li Yuliang and Xie Peide were again elected as vote counters. The vote count showed 10 votes in favor, totaling 858 shares, and 5 votes against, totaling 442 shares. Another majority voted to pass. Shareholders with a special

conflict of interest in the matters of the meeting are not allowed to participate in the vote or act as proxy for other shareholders to exercise their voting rights. Furthermore, if the convening or resolution of the shareholders' meeting violates laws, regulations, or the company's articles of association, the shareholders may, within one month from the date of the resolution, petition the court to declare the resolution invalid. Therefore, in accordance with Articles 131 and 137 of the Company Law, it is requested that Resolutions A and B be declared invalid. The defendant's lawyer, Xu Shihao, then requested that the plaintiff's lawsuit be dismissed, stating that the plaintiff Xie Hengchuan and the defendant Zhang Duchen are both shareholders and directors of the Hua Dong Coal Mine Company. Now, what qualifications does the plaintiff have to file the lawsuit in this case? Furthermore, although the object of the special reward in another lawsuit is currently 150,000 yuan, the plaintiff's lawyer in that case has repeatedly stated that the total special reward is 63 yuan. The filing fee paid by the plaintiff in this case is 4 yuan and 5 jiao, which is inconsistent. The court ordered the case files to be investigated before the retrial.

Thirteen-Year-Old Elementary School Student, Fu Lintao Heroically Saves a Person 149

Rescuing a Qian-Surnamed Child from the Bottom of the River

The Zhengmeng Elementary School in Longwangmiao Town, Pudong, was jointly founded by the Shanghai Jisheng Society and the Shanghai Public Education Practice Association and has been in existence for eleven years. It also serves as a rural service center, providing services such as smallpox vaccinations, medicine distribution, and public speaking, which are highly praised by the villagers. On May 30th of this year, a Qian-surnamed child, seventeen years old, accidentally fell into the Yujia Creek north of the school. A crowd gathered, but everyone was afraid to enter the water to save him because the current was too swift. Fu Lintao, a student at Zhengmeng Elementary School, only thirteen years old, passed by and witnessed the situation. He immediately jumped into the water and, after more than ten minutes, dragged the Qian child out of the river. The Qian child was already unconscious. After being rescued by the crowd, he finally came back to life. It was later learned that the Qian child was the only son of three families. The grief and gratitude of his parents cannot be described. Fu Lintao, Mr. Yi Jun, and Principal Ni Zijia decided to reward Fu, take his photo and hang it in the school, and inscribe the words "Righteousness and Courage" to encourage others.

Yan Yuying Appeals to Liu Dongbao to Restore Mother-Son Relationship 150

Dismissed by the Court, Yan Prepares to Appeal

Liu Chengru, a wealthy man from Nanxun, enjoyed a life of pleasure in his prime. Around the founding of the Republic, under the encouragement of a Mr. Shan Tao, he redeemed a famous prostitute, Ms. Yan, also known as Yuying, from her profession and took her as a concubine. Unexpectedly, she was not accepted by his legal wife, so Liu took advantage of an official appointment to Qingdao to build a golden house for her. Before long this was discovered, and Liu's wife came to Qingdao as well. She was very jealous of Dongbao, the son born to Yan, and forced Liu and Yan to return to Shanghai. From then on, Yan was increasingly mistreated. Unable to endure this, Yan left and went north alone, resuming her previous occupation in Tianjin and was unfortunately arrested by the local police. Upon hearing the news in Shanghai, Liu was moved by the old feelings and, unable to stand by, still enlisted Ye Shantao to rescue her from Tianjin. She then returned to Shanghai and lived in Yide Lane, Zhejiang Road. It was thought that with the legal wife and the concubine living separately, as Yin and Xing avoided each other, they could live in peace. Unexpectedly, Liu's feelings had changed from love to dislike, and eventually, they had to separate. Both parties signed a separation agreement. To cut off all ties and prevent future disputes, Liu stated in the agreement that Dongbao was not born to Yan. At that time, Yan refused to agree to this clause, as this would mean permanently severing her mother-son relationship with Dongbao. However, after repeated persuasion by Ye Shantao, she was told that when Dongbao grew up, there was no reason why a biological son would not recognize his biological mother. If she insisted on her opinion now, the 8,000 yuan in alimony would become a mirage. As she desperately needed money at the time, she had no choice but to accept the mediator's proposal. Thus, mother and son became strangers. Last year, Liu Chengru passed away, and Dongbao is now an adult. Yan recalled Ye Shantao's words and, considering the deep bond between mother and son, requested Dongbao to restore their mother-son relationship. Unexpectedly, Dongbao refused. Helpless, she filed a lawsuit with the First Special District Court, requesting that the clause in the separation agreement stating that there was no mother-son relationship between her and Dongbao be declared invalid. However, the defendant used the agreement as a defense, resulting in the loss of the first trial. Yan refused to accept this outcome and appealed to the Second Branch of the High Court. Ye Shantao and Chen Yuxiang were both summoned to testify. Chen testified that Liu Chengru had indeed told him before his death that Dongbao was born to Yan. Ye, however, testified that he had only heard Yan say that Liu Dongbao was her son and did not provide any details about the

past events. After the arguments were made, the case was declared and dismissed. Yan's depression remained unresolved and she is preparing to appeal to the Supreme Court, hoping to reverse the situation and reunite with her son.

Arguing Over Two Copper Coins, Li Guoyou Was Kicked to Death 151

The Murderer, Wang Dalong, Was Arrested on the Spot

At the end of Linping Road Bridge in Zhabei, at around 6 p.m. the day before yesterday, a vendor, Li Guoyou (from Yancheng, 43 years old, residing in a thatched hut in Fenshui Temple), was arguing with a worker from a yarn factory, Wang Dalong (from Funing, 25 years old, also residing in a thatched hut in Fenshui Temple), over two copper coins for buying broad beans. They began to fight, and Li was fatally injured by punches, his testicles were kicked and crushed. He died on the spot. The murderer, Wang Dalong, was seized by the deceased's daughter, Li Zhaodi (22 years old), and reported to the police for detention. The deceased's wife, Mrs. Huang (39 years old), said that she had an elderly mother-in-law and four children, who depended on her husband for a living. She was deeply saddened by his tragic death. Yesterday afternoon at 4:40 p.m., the District Court sent prosecutor Kong Xianglin and clerk Wang Zhenxin, along with bailiffs, to the scene to examine the body. Mrs. Li Huang, Li Zhaodi, and many other male and female relatives of Li were wailing and crying incessantly, shouting injustice. The police rushed to maintain order before examining the body. The deceased's mouth was frothing with blood, his body was covered with purple bruises, and blood was flowing from his left testicle. Prosecutor Kong then stated that the deceased had indeed died from his injuries. He then got into his car to return to the court, but Mrs. Li Huang and others blocked his way. After being persuaded by the bailiffs, Prosecutor Kong promised to severely punish the murderer before they were able to get rid of the situation. The police station considered the case to be a murder, and yesterday they have handed over the murderer Wang Dalong to the General Bureau for interrogation.

Entire Soybean Curd Industry Resumes Business and Raises Prices Yesterday 154

New Price List to Be Implemented on June 1st

The soybean curd industry in the city has resumed business in its entirety starting yesterday, and the Soybean Curd Industry Association has resolved to raise prices and implement a new price list from June 1st. The association's announcement is recorded as follows: "We, the soybean curd industry, are all small businesses. In recent years, with the decline in the market, maintaining business has been difficult. Since the currency system reform, the cost of raw materials has increased sharply, but the retail price has remained the same, resulting in many businesses closing down. Therefore, the association convened a general meeting of all members on April 29th and resolved to increase prices appropriately to maintain capital. An Obscene Lawsuit in the Buddhist Community 158

A Maid Accuses a Monk of Xuebao Temple of Seduction and Rape - Acquitted After Genital Examination

Miao Hui, the abbot of the Xue Dou Temple branch in Dong Youheng Road, dismissed his employed maid, Lu Liu, after which she filed a lawsuit with the First Special District Court, criminally accusing Miao Hui of seducing, raping, and impregnating her. Furthermore, she accused Lang Qing, a monk from the same temple, of secretly administering abortifacient medicine under the guise of treating her illness, resulting in a miscarriage. She requested that they be punished. After repeated summons and trials, the defendants vehemently denied the seduction and abortion charges. They hired lawyer Hong Shihao to defend them, arguing that the plaintiff was fabricating the charges to deceive and extort. The judge, seeing that both parties' statements were contradictory and fearing difficulty in ascertaining the truth, Lu Liu unexpectedly declared that she knew Miao Hui's genitals were unusually small, which she could not know unless they had shared a bed. Hearing this, Miao Hui admitted that his genitals were large. Therefore, the judge ordered the defendant to be examined by a forensic doctor. However, determining the size of this object was difficult to standardize, so the forensic doctor had to draw a picture of Miao Hui's private parts as they were, with the size exactly as it was. Thus, the truth of the case became clear. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Huang announced the verdict that both Miao Hui and Lang Qing were not guilty.

All Groups and Associations Request a Thorough Investigation into the Wang Xiaolai Slander Case 159

Xin Sheng News Agency reports that over a hundred groups and associations, including the Shanghai Provisional Municipal Council, Local Association, Municipal Education Association, Municipal Farmers' Association, Municipal Federation of Trade Unions, Municipal Chamber of Commerce, Taxpayers' Association, the First and Second Special District City Associations, and various trade associations and citizen branches, have submitted petitions to seven institutions regarding the Wang Xiaolai slander case, including the Central Executive Committee, Shanghai Municipal Executive Committee, Executive Yuan, Control Yuan, Judicial Yuan, Ministry of Industry, and Shanghai Municipal Government, requesting a thorough investigation in accordance with the law. The petition stated: "Submitting a petition for a thorough investigation to rectify public opinion and uphold the righteous spirit of the nation and society. On May 14th, the Shanghai newspapers published an advertisement by Wang Xiaolai, stating, 'Xiaolai has served society for nearly thirty years, with a sincere heart of self-love and patriotism, and an aspiration to save the country. In dealing with people and affairs, I am sincere and fair. In my roles in various social organizations, I have always encouraged myself with the words, "My virtue is insufficient to convince people, and my talent is insufficient to adapt to changes." Since the establishment of the Shanghai Fish Market, Xiaolai has been publicly elected as the general manager. As it concerns industry, I do not shirk from hard work and complaints. What comforts me is that I did not seek this position, nor do I rely on it for a living. Unexpectedly, a so-called Shanghai Federation of Industrial and Commercial Associations has widely distributed leaflets, arbitrarily slandering me. Based on the facts, it is clear. Xiaolai has always been upright. Occasionally, in presiding over social affairs, I have promoted and demoted personnel, causing resentment. But Xiaolai is unashamed and has a clear conscience. Having lived in Shanghai for thirty years, I have never accepted illicit gains and remain penniless, which is known to all. As for the address and responsible person of the Shanghai Federation of Industrial and Commercial Associations printed on the leaflet with a "needle" mark, I am willing to meet them face to face and publicly question them. I, Xiaolai, should conduct a thorough investigation to seek legal sanctions. I hereby declare this plainly, hoping for public consideration.' Since the publication of the advertisement, several days have passed, and no responsible person from the so-called Shanghai Federation of Industrial and Commercial Associations has stepped forward to meet Wang Xiaolai, causing even more unease among the people of Shanghai. Since the New Life Movement, propriety, justice, integrity, and shame have become the prevailing ethos, and the punishment of corruption has become the law. Wang Xiaolai holds an important position. If there are any misdeeds as claimed by the so-called Shanghai Federation of Industrial and Commercial Associations, they should be thoroughly investigated in accordance with the law. We should not let it go unpunished. The law has specific provisions for those who make false accusations. Since this matter involves responsible personnel in society, the government should conduct a rigorous investigation to protect the righteous spirit of society and families, punish those who undermine discipline, and commend those who are upright and selfless. This will rectify public opinion and maintain law and order. Therefore, we earnestly petition for a review of Wang Xiaolai's conduct and request a prompt and thorough investigation in accordance with the law, without leniency or injustice, and without errors. Society will be fortunate, and the nation will be fortunate. We are sincerely grateful."

Three Trafficking Cases Cracked Inside the Huashan Maru 162

The trend of luring and kidnapping children is rampant. On the 22nd of last month, four children were kidnapped on Rue de Coullers in the French Concession, and three children were kidnapped on Rue de Conthay. Seven children were lost in a single day, which is truly shocking. It is said that the child traffickers sell the kidnapped children to Xiamen and Shantou, where each child can be sold for 100 to 150 yuan. At 9:00 AM yesterday, Chen Shaoting and Lin Yongfang, investigators from the China Women and Children Relief Association, together with customs water police detectives Qu He Kui and Xu Juelu, went to the third-class cabin of the Japanese Qing Company's Huashan Maru, which was berthed at the old pier in the east of the Bund, and cracked three trafficking cases. Chen Jinkui from Chaozhou and his concubine Chen Aying from Dingxi jointly kidnapped a six-year-old Ningbo child named Kong Ximin. Yang Yao, a woman from Pudong (also known as Sanmei), lured and kidnapped an eleven-year-old Chuansha girl named Zhou Lindi. Chen Along from Wenzhou and his concubine Chen Xie from Guangdong jointly kidnapped a six-year-old Shandong child named Changsheng. The cases were exposed due to contradictions in the statements between the traffickers and the children. All eight individuals, adults and children, were taken to the water police station for separate interrogations. Chen Jinkui and Chen Aying confessed that they lived in the attic on the third floor of No. 98 Rue Massenet in the French Concession. On the eighth day of the first lunar month, they, along with accomplices Gong Zhengming (also known as A Ming) and Wang A'er, kidnapped three boys in Shanghai and took the Huashan Maru to Xiamen, where they earned 330 yuan. The second time was on the ninth day of the third lunar month, when they kidnapped another boy and also took the Huashan Maru to Xiamen, earning 190 yuan. This was their third time. Gong Zhengming first kidnapped a girl named Zhou Lindi, and then Yang Yao kidnapped Kong Ximin. They were hidden in their attic on the third floor, waiting to be shipped out of the country. According to Yang Yao's confession, she still tried to deny it. According to the joint confessions of Chen Along and Chen Xie, they insisted that the child Changgen was their own, but Changgen spoke with a Shandong accent, which was clearly untrue. According to the girl Zhou Lindi, her parents lived on Rue Pichon. Kong Ximin said that his father was deceased, his mother was alive, and they lived in Shou'anfang on Baoshan Road in Zhabei. When Changgen was questioned, he did not answer the questions, only saying that his father sold fish, and he knew nothing else. The detectives rushed to arrest the fugitives Gong Zhengming and Wang A'er, but they had already fled upon hearing the news. They also went to Rue Pichon to find the family of the girl Zhou Lindi. When they found the destination, families who had lost children at that location came to inquire about the whereabouts of their children. For a moment, both Rue Pichon and Rue de Conthay were in an uproar, with over a hundred onlookers gathering to see the faces of the traffickers the detectives were bringing. Some even pointed and scolded them. The detectives took the family of Zhou Lindi to the station to identify the faces and, after confirming they were correct, waited to escort the traffickers and children to the Shanghai District Court for interrogation this morning before returning them.

On January 28th, Wang Bao instructed the plaintiff to go to room 447 of the East Asia Hotel on Nanjing Road to look for her. Unexpectedly, upon entering, he was forced to sign a divorce agreement by more than ten hooligans who had been gathered beforehand. Since then, the plaintiff has been unfortunate and suffering from illness, currently residing in a relative's home. Therefore, he requested that the divorce agreement be confirmed as invalid and demanded to live together. Wang Miaohe did not attend, but Wang Bao and her daughter Wang Caibao attended and stated that Wang Yousheng did not engage in honest work, but was engaged in vagrancy. When he had no money, he would go home to cause trouble, forcefully demanding money to spend outside. If he was not satisfied, he would destroy the furniture and beat his wife. At the end of the lunar year, he forced his wife to hand over the land deed for mortgage, and when he was unsuccessful, he beat his wife with his fists and feet. Unable to endure the abuse, she temporarily stayed at her sister's house to avoid his attacks. Seeing that his demands were not met, the plaintiff invited Mr. Wang, an employee of the British American Tobacco Company, to discuss the divorce, asking for 500 yuan. Later, they agreed on 200 yuan and signed the divorce agreement. Of all the money, 100 yuan was cash, and 100 yuan was used to offset the deposit of the tea house at the Continental Hotel. It was the plaintiff who requested the divorce. Having already divorced, it would be difficult to reconcile. They requested that the lawsuit be dismissed. The court considered that it was necessary to summon witnesses in this case and adjourned the hearing.

Fire at Hengyuchang Paper Store on Rue des Soeurs 172

The Hengyuchang Paper Store at No. 848 Rue des Soeurs, South City, was opened by Wang Yushan from Ningbo (28 years old). He ran a small business, and his livelihood was fairly sustainable. At around 2:20 AM yesterday morning, a certain apprentice at the store, due to the late hour, was cooking a midnight meal to satisfy his hunger. Inadvertently, he left the fire unattended, and sparks shot out, with black smoke like ink. The fire became uncontrollable and quickly broke through the roof, spreading to the adjacent Wang family's residence at No. 846. Fire trucks from various fire brigades in the South City rushed to the scene to put out the fire. It took about an hour to extinguish the flames. As a result, two houses were burned down. The arsonist was detained by police officers at the Gaochang Temple Police Substation to investigate the cause of the fire. It is reported that the store had fire insurance of 1,000 yuan.

Bank of China Inspection Report 175

Based on regulations, this committee inspected the Shanghai Bank of China's head office and its branches regarding the special reserve for issuing and redeeming banknotes. On May 31, 1936, under the leadership of Dai Mingli, Director of the Currency Department of the Ministry of Finance, along with representatives from the Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce, Wang Yansong and Pei Yunqing; representatives from the Shanghai Banking Association, Qu Jigang and Zhuang Dezhi; representatives from the Shanghai Money Trade Association, Liu Wuqiao and Zhang Wenbo; representatives from banknote-receiving banks and firms, Chen Guangfu and Hu Disheng; representatives from the Bank of China's board of directors and supervisors, Chen Guangfu, Xu Jilou, and Li Zhilian, and in conjunction with accountant Wang Zikang, the 99th inspection was conducted at the bank. The inspection results are listed below:

Total value of banknotes issued: 23,004,317.79 yuan, including:

- Value of banknotes issued by the head office: 13,240,124.42 yuan

- Value of banknotes received by branches: 6,991,694.20 yuan

- Value of banknotes received by other banks and firms: 2,772,499.50 yuan

Total value of banknote reserves: 23,004,317.79 yuan, including:

- Cash reserves: 15,259,232.87 yuan

- Guarantee reserves: 7,745,085.03 yuan

The cash reserves accounted for 60% and the guarantee reserves accounted for 40%, which were all verified to be accurate.

This is a formal report. May 31, 1936.

Establishment of the World Literature Institute 178

The Shanghai World Literature Correspondence College is the most complete academic institution in China. Established three years ago, it has achieved remarkable results, with students all over the country and abroad, reaching more than a thousand people. The college decided last year to expand its plan, burying itself in improvements, and striving to meet social requirements. Recently, major cultural institutions have been assisting each other and refreshing their internal structures, raising funds, and deciding to expand into the World Literature Research Institute. A correspondence department will be established, and 20 writers will be hired to host teaching. The institute's address has been set at 429 Songbai Road in this city. It is said that the institute is determined to proceed and will soon be established. In the future, the institute will completely focus on modern literature and art. The Shanghai Literature Correspondence College will be responsible for the old Chinese literature. Recently, the institute hosted various circles to report on its establishment.

"Heaven, Earth, and Man" Issue 7 Published: The seventh issue of the bi-monthly "Heaven, Earth, and Man" published by the Independent Publishing House was published on June 1st. Its content is rich, the materials are practical, the posture is new, and the attitude is kind, providing readers with spiritual and intellectual needs. The retail price is 15 cents per issue. It includes Xu Qinwen's "Xiaotaoyuan Diary", Wang Kongjia's translation of "Mrs. Jia Tailai's Lover", a short essay by Qu Yuan from social instinct to national salvation, Xu Yu's "Talking about Human Suffering", A Ding's "The Content and Comparison of the Four Travel Notes", Chen Yuncong's "Minbian", the story of Jinfa studying abroad, and other short articles, Zhou Ziya's European correspondence "After Addis Ababa was captured" and "Is the Balkan Alliance possible?", A Yu's "The Story of Painting" and other casual talks, Xu Yu's "Poetry", Hua Mu's "Puppet Show in Meixian", and other folk literature. The total number of words is more than 80,000. It is published by the Independent Publishing House at 380 Fuzhou Road, Shanghai, and distributed by the China Book and Magazine Company.

"Great Wall Monthly" Volume 3, Issue 12 Published: This magazine is edited by Pan Wen'an and is known for discussing work and self-cultivation. It is the only magazine of its kind in China. The content of this issue includes "On Unity", "Coldness", "Talking about Changing Minds", "Behavioral Control", Business Sutras, "Ten Points that Salesmen Should Pay Attention To", "Close at Hand, Far Away", "A Visit to Mr. Tang Huaiqiu", etc., which are worth reading. The magazine welcomes readers to try it out. Send a letter to the Great Wall Monthly Magazine at 17 Ningbo Road, Shanghai, with one cent for postage, and it will be sent immediately.

"He and She" Reprinted: Ms. Hua Luochen, originally from Poland, studied in France and married Mr. Hua Tongzhai from our country, so she calls China her second motherland. This time, she revisited Shanghai, and the leaders of the women's circle in this city specially held a banquet at the China Women's Production Cooperative to welcome her and to offer her a cleansing ceremony. The lady is good at literature, especially at writing novels. Her published works include "Love and Obligation" (Chinese, English, and two French versions), "He and She", "Double Practice", and the essay collection "Xinwen", all published by the Commercial Press and popular for a time. Among them, "He and She" has been sold out for a long time and has now been reprinted. The content narrates a woman who meets a bad person, angrily studies in Europe, and when she returns to China after completing her studies, her husband has realized and reformed his ways, and the estranged couple becomes a happy couple. The purpose is to criticize the society of our country, which is different from ordinary novels that only write about joys and sorrows. The price per book is 20 cents.

Weather Report 187

The Xujiahui Observatory's weather forecast at 4:30 PM yesterday stated that the mountains and surrounding areas are sunny and sandy, with strong northwest breezes. The middle reaches of the Yangtze River and the Hankou area are cloudy and gradually overcast, with variable wind directions. The lower reaches of the Yangtze River and this area are cloudy and hot, but still sunny, with southeast to southwest winds. The East China Sea and Taiwan are overcast with rain, and there are northeast to southeast winds. Also, in the 24 hours before 3:00 PM yesterday, the highest temperature in this area was 87.1 degrees and the lowest was 63.9 degrees. On the same day last year, the highest was 81.1 degrees and the lowest was 63.5 degrees.

Educational News

Ministry of Education Plans to Formulate Expanded Literacy Education Plan 188

Promoting Civil Schools Compulsory Training

(Nanjing, 1st dispatch) The Ministry of Education is planning to formulate an expanded literacy education plan and has issued a circular to all provinces and cities to implement it earnestly from 1936. 1. Promote people's schools and compel people to organize training. The people will be from 15 to 30 years old, and then extended to 40 years old. Those who do not receive training will be severely punished. 2. In terms of teachers, each province and city will set up a people's education cadre training class. 3. In terms of curriculum, in addition to literacy training and civic training, self-defense training will be added.

Shanghai Branch of the Cultural Construction Association Preparing for Invention Exhibition Exhibition Methods Announced Yesterday

The Shanghai Branch of the Cultural Construction Association is hosting an exhibition of inventions from China in the past ten years. The preparatory committee held its second preparatory meeting yesterday. More than ten people attended, including Dong Hangbai, Jiang Jianbai, He Bingsong, Wu Huanru, Zhang Shuliang, Hu Duanxing, Huang Jingzhai, Zhou Hanmei, and Tian Heqing. Several important cases were discussed and decided. The association's adopted methods for the exhibition of inventions in the past ten years are recorded as follows: Chapter 1 General Principles, Article 1 The Shanghai Branch of the Chinese Cultural Construction Association is holding an exhibition of inventions in the past ten years in order to promote new inventions and encourage future generations. Article 2 The association will form a preparatory committee to be responsible for all preparation and exhibition work. Its organizational rules will be determined separately. Article 3 The preparatory office of this association is located at 500 Lafayette Road, Shanghai, the location of this branch. Chapter 2 Collection of Items, Article 4 The items collected by this association will mainly be various inventions related to culture in our country in the past ten years. All other new discoveries or improvements with cultural value will also be collected. Article 5 The exhibitors are limited to citizens of the Republic of China and their self-run institutions. The scope of the collection is divided into the following five categories: A. New inventions, B. New discoveries, C. All items whose quality or manufacturing method has been improved in the past ten years and has achieved significant results, D. Those who first imitated foreign products and were approved by government agencies, E. Inventions or new discoveries before ten years that have made great contributions to culture. Article 6 The items collected by this association are divided into the following four categories: Humanities category: All new discoveries related to the legacy of our country's ancestors, national life, and culture (those who have made considerable contributions to human evolutionary history), and various new inventions or discoveries related to writing, language, education. Agricultural category: All items related to farming, gardening, animal husbandry, animal husbandry, fishery, afforestation, and other rural sideline occupations. Industrial category: All products related to all manufacturing industries such as machinery manufacturing, metal product manufacturing, electrical appliance manufacturing, transportation equipment manufacturing, stone product manufacturing, construction engineering, chemical industry, textile industry (cotton, wool, silk, hemp, etc.), clothing product manufacturing, rubber industry (rubber products and leather products), food industry, printing and papermaking industry, specimen instrument industry, and other daily necessities manufacturing industries. Art category: All equipment related to painting, calligraphy, sculpture, embroidery, film, drama, sports (sports equipment), music, toys, etc. Article 7 Anyone who has made an invention or discovery in theory, practice, or method that cannot be expressed in kind may send a written explanation of the theory or method to the meeting for display. Article 8 All kinds of collected items sent to this association for display are mainly original objects. If it is unavoidable, models or photographs may be made and sent to this association for display. Article 9 Whether the exhibitor is an institution, group, company, firm, or individual, they must fill out the two types of instruction manuals A and B printed by the association, sign and seal them, and send them directly to the association. Article 10 After receiving the product instruction manual, the association will notify the exhibitor to transport it to the association on a regular basis after passing the review. The shipping cost will be borne by the exhibitor. Article 11 The collection date of this association is from June 1, 1936 to August 10. Chapter 3 Exhibition, Article 12 The location of the exhibition of this association will be determined separately. Article 13 This association is scheduled to open the exhibition on October 1, 1936. The duration of the exhibition is half a month and may be extended if necessary. Article 14 The location of the exhibition of items will be determined by this association. If the item requires special installation, the exhibitor should first draw up a drawing and send it to this association for reference. The installation and expenses will be borne by the exhibitor. Article 15 Anyone who wants to sell displayed items must mark the actual price. If someone orders it, the money and goods will be exchanged at the closing, and one-tenth of the proceeds will be used for the association's expenses, and nine-tenths will be remitted to the exhibitor. Chapter 4 Examination and Awards, Article 16 The association will separately hire experts to form an examination committee to be responsible for identifying and evaluating the various inventions according to the types of displayed items. Article 17 All kinds of inventions sent to this association for display must be examined and approved by the examination committee before they can be displayed. Article 18 After the exhibition of various displayed items is completed, the examination committee will evaluate the size of the inventions' contribution to culture and give various awards according to the level of the inventions: (1) This association will submit a request to the central government for commendation. (2) This association will issue medals, certificates, and awards. (3) This association will publish a commemorative special issue for wide promotion. Article 19 The awards in the preceding paragraph will be given to the inventor or inventing institution listed in the product instruction manual. Chapter 5 Supplementary Provisions, Article 20 This association is fully responsible for all protection of items, except for damage or incompleteness during transportation that is noted on the receipt and in the register. However, it is not responsible for compensation for damage caused by force majeure. Article 21 This association welcomes those who are willing to keep the items after the exhibition period for permanent display. Article 22 The various rules and forms of this association will be determined separately.

Scheduled to be held in Chengdu starting August 16th, Methods for soliciting proposals and papers announced yesterday

The 16th Annual Meeting of the China Vocational Education Society and the 10th National Vocational Education Conference are scheduled to be held in Chengdu, Sichuan, from August 16th to 18th. The society has already begun preparations, and the methods for soliciting proposals, reports, and papers have been stipulated as follows: The proposals should follow the following scope: A. Regarding vocational school education: curriculum and teaching materials, student internships, discipline, graduate employment, and graduate service guidance; B. Regarding vocational supplementary education: the widespread promotion of vocational supplementary education, subject setting, and discipline; C. Regarding rural education and rural improvement: educational programs for improving the rural economy, methods for promoting vocational rural primary schools, methods for compiling rural primary school teaching materials, and methods for promoting rural education/improvement at the district or village level; D. Regarding career guidance: methods for training career guidance personnel and promoting career guidance methods; E. Regarding administrative matters: plans for vocational teacher training, the establishment of inspector positions, and effective liaison with all sectors of society; F. Regarding special methods: issues of national rejuvenation education. Proposals must be sent to the Society's office by July 5th for review by the review committee. Late submissions will not be included. All submitted proposals will be reviewed by the review committee, and may be merged. Those deemed unnecessary for discussion may be temporarily retained with an explanation of the reasons. For this meeting, the Society has specially appointed the following individuals to form the review committee: He Bingsong, Ou Yuan Ao, Zhong Daozan, Liu Zhanen, Zhang Yi, Zou Bingwen, Tang Ying, Liao Shicheng, Huang Yanpei, Jiang Hengyuan, Yang Elian, He Qingru, and Pan Wenan. Reports from attending members are divided into the following two types: A. Written reports; B. Oral reports. Members may choose either. Written reports should be sent to the Society by July 5th. If time permits, they may be printed and distributed, otherwise they will be displayed at the venue for viewing. Members intending to give oral reports at the conference should notify the Society in writing by July 5th, along with a summary for the review committee to arrange the order of reports. If the number of speakers is too large, restrictions may be imposed. Members who wish to submit academically valuable papers based on special research are also welcome. These papers should be sent to the Society by June 25th for review by the review committee. The most important papers will be selected for presentation at the conference. The Society plans to organize a conference preparatory committee before the meeting to handle all related matters. The committee members will be publicly elected later.

Great China University's 12th Anniversary Yesterday 198

Great China University has been established for twelve years. Yesterday was the anniversary of the school's founding. All school buildings were opened to welcome visitors, and alumni were invited back to the school on May 31st for a reunion dinner. Details were reported in yesterday's newspaper. It is now learned that a commemorative meeting was held in the gymnasium at 9 AM yesterday. In addition to President Wang Boqun, Vice President Ou Yuanhuai, and professors Wang Zhiwei, Chuan Shishuo, Lu Jihui, Wu Haoran, Shao Jialin, Sun Haodeng, Ren Mengxian, and Lan Chunchi, as well as over 1,600 graduates and students, board members in attendance included Jiang Wenyu, Zhang Zhuping, and Zhao Jinqing. Guests included Director Pan Gongzhan and Jiang Jianbai. The meeting was chaired by President Wang Boqun, who delivered the opening remarks, stating that the school has made significant progress in both material and spiritual terms in a very short time, which is the result of the cooperation of teachers and students. This year's anniversary coincides with a time of national crisis, and no extravagance that would undermine national strength will be undertaken. He expressed the hope that all professors and students would uphold the past spirit of perseverance and hard work, teach and learn diligently, and continue to strive to achieve the goal of revitalizing national education. Vice President Ou Yuanhuai then reported on the school's operations over the past twelve years, stating that the school was established in 1924 by over two hundred students and some professors who left Xiamen University to come to Shanghai. At that time, there was no place to stand, and it was completely like a "congenitally deficient" infant. After its establishment, it experienced many difficulties and setbacks before it could have the rudiments of its current scale, just like a "child with many acquired difficulties." The school's financial difficulties have not yet escaped the state of 1924, and he hoped that all students and people from all walks of life would provide appropriate assistance. Director Pan Gongzhan then delivered a speech with much encouragement, stating that if the school's colleagues could continue the past spirit of teacher-student cooperation and work hard, they would definitely be able to overcome the difficulties. Board members Jiang Wenyu and Zhao Jinqing then delivered speeches, and graduate representative Zhang Zhonghuan delivered a speech. Finally, everyone sang the school song and the meeting adjourned. Guests and board members visited the school's science hall, which has been increasingly enriched in recent years, after the meeting. They were personally guided by Shao Jialin, the dean of the College of Science. In the afternoon, the school's students held friendly ball games with the affiliated high schools of Jinan and Fudan Universities, the School of Taxation, and the China Women's Physical Education College, it is said.

Pan Yuliang's Art Exhibition Opens Today 199

The solo painting exhibition of the famous female painter Ms. Pan Yuliang will open today at the Chinese Art Society on Avenue Amiral Courbet in the French Concession. On display are 200 works of oil paintings, pastels, and figure sketches, mostly recent masterpieces by Ms. Pan from her travels to Nanjing, Beiping, Qingdao, Laoshan, Yandang, Tiantai, Huashan, Putuo, Huangshan, and the scenic spots of Suzhou and Hangzhou. A tea party will be held at the venue at 4 PM today to welcome the literary and artistic circles to visit.

Physical Education Coaches Organize Physical Education Research Association 208

Physical education instructors from various universities in this city had organized a physical education research association twice five or six years ago, but after the organization, there was no news of it. Now, there are those who are launching a so-called physical education research association. After the closing of the 9th Jiangnan University track and field meet, the physical education coaches of various universities in this city gathered at the Huibinlou that evening at the invitation of Zhang Shouyong, the president of Guanghua University. During the dinner, the coaches realized that there was no organization in this city for physical education coaches from various schools to gather, study, and exchange ideas, so they planned to organize a group to contact each other at any time. After some discussion, all those present agreed, and after detailed consultation, the establishment will be announced soon. It is said that the name has been tentatively set as the "Shanghai Physical Education Research Association."

Financial Standard Gold Rises with Customs Gold 213

Market Conditions Initially Firm Then Uncertain, Resulting in a Further Increase of 2.4 Yuan

Yesterday, the gold market was stirred by the reversed rise in Customs Gold, which aroused people's feelings. The market opened with an upward trend, but later, due to multiple parties selling off, the actions of the three banks to force down the exchange rate finally calmed the market. Ultimately, the market was uncertain. Initially, overseas telegrams reported that the US market was completely closed, and that the prices of London's large bars and Montevideo's forward silver rose slightly. Exchange rates decreased slightly, and London's raw gold decreased by half a penny. Over-the-counter preliminary transactions opened at 39.0 yuan, with little trading. The Central Bank's posted price was announced, with the British and American markets remaining stable. The customs gold unit reversed and increased by 0.4%, and the standard gold price was posted at 1132.4 yuan, which made people feel very bullish. Dade Cheng, Chun Yuan, Yong Fu Xing, Yong Qia Feng, Yong Ding Kang, and others all purchased, rising to 42 yuan. Dade Cheng, Yuan Mao, and Yong sold off, dropping by 1 yuan. Fu Xing and Yong Chun Yuan Yong continued to purchase. The morning opening was high. After the opening, people's hearts were uncertain, and the appetites of large investors varied, resulting in uncertainty. After the rise, the market declined, but did not break the 40 yuan mark. Large investors took advantage of the low price to maintain their positions. Although HSBC's posted price was flat, it still rose. Later, as large investors took advantage of the high price to sell off, the market gradually stabilized, and trading also decreased. In the end, due to the sale of floating positions, the overall trend was mediocre at noon, and the market remained uncertain. It once rose after the opening, but due to large investors closing out their positions, it turned to hovering, and there was no special change in the result. Yesterday, the futures spread was posted at 3.45 yuan by multiple parties. The market conditions for today are recorded below:

The morning opening was 1141.4 yuan, an increase of 2.3 yuan compared to last Saturday. Chun Yuan, Yong Yuanmao Yong Dade Cheng Qia Feng Yong came in and out, and the market immediately felt uncertain. Later, Xiang He Heng Chang Yong Chun Yuan Yong Fu Sheng Yong Lai Jin rose from 1.1 yuan to 2.5 yuan. Qia Feng Yong Jiu Da Yuan Mao Yong Chun Yuan Yong Fu Xing Yong Da Dade Cheng Hui Xiang Lian jointly sold off, dropping to 0.2 yuan. Chun Yuan Yong Ding Kang Da Dade Cheng Yuan Mao Yong Heng Chang Yong and others successively purchased bars. Although HSBC's posted price was flat, it still rose to 2.8 yuan. Qia Feng Yong Chun Yuan Da Heng Yuan Mao Yong and others took advantage of the high price to sell, and the balance tax was announced, which decreased by half a point, gradually moving downstream. After this, trading gradually became scarce, and floating positions were also closed out, dropping to 0.7 yuan. The noon closing was 1140.8 yuan.

The afternoon market opened at 1140.9 yuan. Heng Chang Yong Heng Yu Hui Xiang advanced to 2 yuan. Tong Tai Chang Fu Xing Yong Hui Xiang Heng Yu Ding Kang sold off, retreating to 1.2 yuan. Dade Cheng Heng Yu Tong Yi Li Tai Yong Tong Yu Run entered and exited, rising to 1.7 yuan. Yi Cheng sold late, and then retreated to 1.2 yuan. After fluctuating, the closing price was 1141.5 yuan.

The settlement price was posted by the Central Bank at 1132.4 yuan, which, according to the closing price, was raised by more than 9 yuan, and by less than 3 yuan compared to last Saturday. The registration for this month is 1137 yuan, and for July it is 1141 yuan. The water supplement in the morning was 1137 yuan, and in the afternoon it was 1138 yuan. The standard gold was increased by 5 yuan to 1146.8 yuan. The spot market was stable. Tianjin goods were increased by 11 yuan, and roasted gold was increased by 10 yuan, but there were no sellers. Yesterday, the futures spread was given to Ying Feng Heng by Qia Feng Yong for 14 bars, at 3.5 yuan, and by Yuan Mao Yong for 7 bars, at 3.4 yuan.

There was not much trading in the market. In summary, Heng Chang Yong Da Fa Yong Shun Mao Qing Fa Yong Xiang He Heng Yu Yong De Qian Chang Xiang Fu Xing Yong Xiang Feng and others were on the selling side, and Yuan Mao Yong Qing Xiang Da Dade Cheng Qia Feng Yong Tong Feng Heng Yi Cheng Fu Tai Yong and others were on the selling side. Yu Xin Xiang advanced and then retreated, and Shen Da Yong Chun Yuan Yong retreated and then advanced.

Checking the day's market conditions, the morning opening was 241.4 yuan, and the final closing was 1141.5 yuan. The highest was 1142.8 yuan, and the lowest was 1140.6 yuan, with a fluctuation of 2.6 yuan. As a result, it rose by 2.4 yuan compared to last Saturday. There are only 350 bars left for this month's public bonds, totaling 10 long positions and 2 short positions. The total number of chips for July is 11,536, totaling 46 long positions and 34 short positions. The total number of transactions was 6,125 in the morning session and 1,400 in the afternoon session.

The only short position for public bonds that was settled yesterday was Ying Feng Heng with 42 bars. Today's long positions to be closed are: Yi Cheng with 14 bars, and Tong Feng Heng Fu Tai Heng Da Dade Cheng Qia Feng Yong each with 7 bars. The settlement price is 1137 yuan.

Foreign Exchange Buying Frenzy Remains Intense 214

The Three Banks Strive to Offer Supply, Exchange Market Sees Little Change

Yesterday, although foreign and Chinese businesses bought actively on the exchange market, it remained generally stable due to the banks' efforts to adjust. Early in the morning, news from overseas markets indicated that London spot exchange had risen nearly 0.0625, with no changes in forward rates. It was said that buyers were satisfied. The Montreal forward silver price remained unchanged, at 6.06 or thereabouts. The U.S. market was closed for the holiday. London gold was down half a penny, the British pound against the U.S. dollar fell 0.1875, and the British pound against the French franc fell three points. The Central Bank's official rates were announced, with both the British pound and the U.S. dollar unchanged. The Customs Gold Unit rose 0.04.

The exchange market opened in the morning with the spot selling price for the British pound at 1 shilling, 2 pence, 0.375, and the U.S. dollar at 29.875 yuan. Compared to last Saturday, the British pound was unchanged while the U.S. dollar was up 0.0625. After the opening, due to Sin Fung Foreign Exchange actively buying spot pounds and Chinese businesses actively buying U.S. dollars, the situation tightened. However, the Bank of China released spot pounds and other banks offered U.S. dollars. When the Yien Yieh Bank announced its official rates, with both the British pound and the U.S. dollar unchanged, the market began to fluctuate. The silver equalization tax was announced, up half a cent, with little impact. As the day progressed, the situation gradually stabilized, although foreign firms continued to actively buy U.S. dollars. The afternoon trading pattern was set, with banks trading among themselves. Although some firms bought spot pounds, the Bank of China continued to adjust, stabilizing the trend. Furthermore, Shanghai continued to offer U.S. dollars, resulting in even less change. By the close of trading, the spot selling price for the British pound was 1 shilling, 2 pence, 0.375, and the U.S. dollar was 29.875 yuan. Compared to the previous close, the British pound was unchanged while the U.S. dollar was up 0.0625. The forward rates were the same. Chinese businesses bought over 300,000 U.S. dollars, and foreign firms also actively traded. Today's trading records are listed below:

Securities: Northern Faction Selling Securities 215

—Continuous Decline for a Week… A Rebound May Occur

Yesterday, the selling pressure intensified on the Chinese Merchant Securities Exchange as market prices continued to fall. This was due to the situation in North China, with Japanese troops continuously entering China. The current situation is of extreme importance. The Northern Faction in the market showed signs of panic, leading to a significant amount of government bonds being sold. However, most people remain steadfast. Current news and developments are significantly influencing the market. However, after a week of continuous price declines, a rebound should be anticipated.

Yesterday, the downward trend was evident from the opening of the morning session. The November 11th contract saw consistent selling, with Class D forward contracts falling sharply by 0.06 yuan, and other contracts also declining by 0.03 or 0.05 yuan. Contracts 47 and 18 were also sold off. Contract 4 also saw more selling than buying. At the close, although retail investors and those holding Contract 4 had some demand, the market was unable to recover due to the heavy selling pressure from the Northern Faction and those holding contracts 5 and 10. Therefore, even though prices were slightly better by 0.01 or 0.02 yuan before the opening, the sentiment was dampened again after Contract A forward fell by 0.04 yuan due to selling by number 14. At the close, only Class B forward contracts saw a slight rebound of 0.015 yuan, while the rest remained weak. Although there were over 100,000 shares of Class A forward sold by number 14, the market only fell by 0.005 yuan. Despite the strong downward pressure, major long positions did not appear to be liquidating in large quantities.

As a result, Class D forward contracts fell the most, declining by 0.08 yuan, while Class A spot contracts fell the least, declining by 0.035 yuan. The total transaction volume was 63,600 yuan. The yarn market is trending weaker, showing a slight downturn. This is due to the deteriorating situation in North China, which has weakened market sentiment. Prices are depressed, but major players have not yet taken action, so the decline is relatively moderate. The November yarn futures market is mostly bearish, and short sellers are becoming active again. Sales of spot yarn by the Sichuan clique are still good.

Price of Traded Yarn Falls Step by Step

In the morning session for traded yarn, prices for different months varied. They rose or fell by 0.04 or 0.05 yuan. Indian cotton performed well. Later, due to poor market sentiment, Chang Feng, Sheng Yuan, Xin Cheng, etc., continued to sell, but De Da bought in large quantities. However, this still could not curb the selling pressure. As a result, prices for each month fell by 0.03, 0.07, or 0.09 yuan compared to the previous day's closing price. This month alone fell by 1.13 yuan. In the afternoon session, the market was still dominated by rumors, and prices fell step by step. The September and October contracts broke through the 200 yuan level. Indian Cotton Soars, Traded Cotton Still Weak After Initial Strength 217

—Due to Weak Yarn Market and Falling Expectations for New Cotton—

The cotton market initially strengthened but then weakened, and the situation is deteriorating. Due to the weak yarn market and persistent negative sentiment, many long positions were liquidated. Furthermore, the recent favorable weather conditions have led to widespread expectations of falling prices for new cotton. However, the strength of Indian cotton is exceptionally strong. July and August white cotton prices have reached 209 rupees.

New Cotton Prospects are Poor

Oil Market: Shanghai and Hankou Tung Oil Inventory Gradually Dwindling 229

Selling Prices Standing Above 70 Yuan Per Dan

After tung oil prices in the Hankou market rose above 70 yuan per dan, they have stabilized. Although they once reached a high of 78 yuan, they quickly fell back and have been fluctuating between 72 and 73 yuan. Two weeks ago, the market rumored that there would be government control, so prices briefly fell to 69 yuan, but this was only a fleeting occurrence, and prices quickly returned above 70 yuan. Recently, there have been rumors that the United States will increase the import tax on tung oil, and there are varying opinions on whether prices will rise or fall, so the market has not been affected. Because tung oil is a unique product of our country and the United States has the largest demand, even if the output increases annually, it is still not enough to meet the needs of the world. Currently, 70-80% of the production in various producing areas has been sold. The remaining inventory is only enough to supply the market for five months. With monthly exports of over 5,000 tons, it is feared that it will only be enough to last for three months. As a result, there will be no supply for two months. Therefore, the current market price above 70 yuan is not surprising. When the old crop is exhausted and the new crop is not yet available, there may be even more surprising price increases. Before the new crop was produced last year, old oil was sold for 87 yuan. The situation is even tighter this year, so it is feared that the price will be even higher than that.

However, it is now heard that the Ministry of Industry has established a vegetable oil factory to improve export trade and will not allow similar oil factories to operate. Bao tung oil exports must be inspected and qualified by the Commodity Inspection Bureau before they can be shipped. Therefore, tung oil exports have already been improved. It is heard that oil merchants in the Sichuan, Hunan, and Hubei provinces have jointly petitioned the government, demanding that the order be withdrawn. Oil merchants in Jiangsu and Zhejiang are still waiting and seeing.

Metals: Narrow Strip Steel Market Active 230

The recent market for narrow strip steel has been active due to the rising prices of tinplate. Many users have switched to using narrow strip steel. Although market volume has not increased, its popularity is not comparable to other metal products. The current market price is 22.5 yuan per box (calculated at 200 pounds). It is found that there were as many as four or five hundred boxes offered on the market yesterday, mostly purchased by canning factories, cigarette factories, and paint companies. Wholesalers also made some purchases.

Thin Sheet Inventory Drops Dramatically 231

Thin sheets, which are necessary for cigarette companies and biscuit factories, have repeatedly reported price increases overseas in recent months. Therefore, few merchants have placed orders because they cannot profit. Recently, Shantou merchants and local factories have all purchased, so market goods have become scarce. Standard, good quality sheets have increased by several yuan. The current price is 68 yuan per box. However, buyers are still purchasing despite the high prices. Twenty-five boxes were offered yesterday.
